Southwestern Authorities Issue a Circular Telegram Refuting the Report of the Investigation Team

Stating that the Investigation Team Abandoned Its Founding Convention and Recognized Facts

The Northeast Problem Can Only Be Resolved Through National Strength 24

Guangzhou The Southwest Executive Department of the National Government and the Southwest Political Affairs Committee issued a circular stating: All newspaper offices are aware that since the September 18th Incident, the authorities have not attempted to resist, but relied on the League of Nations. Japan has disregarded the League of Nations, repeatedly ordering the withdrawal of troops, and actively expanding its scope of aggression. It is not heard that the League of Nations has taken effective measures in accordance with the covenant. Instead, in the face of facts seen and heard by the world, it has used the dispatch of an investigation team to delay the matter, thereby allowing Japanese warlords to act recklessly. They have subjected our Shanghai and Songjiang areas to unprecedented devastation and have used the old tricks of annexing Korea in our Northeast to create puppet organizations. Recently, they have brazenly recognized these puppet organizations and have unilaterally established treaties equivalent to annexation. It is not heard that the League of Nations has offered a single word of correction. Our country has suffered such deep and great trauma, yet we are still concealing our grievances, waiting for the completion of the investigation team's work, hoping that the League of Nations will base its report on a fair resolution. Unexpectedly, yesterday, after reading the newspaper, the summary of the investigation team's report, which was announced on the 1st of this month, the team proposed so-called basic principles and methods that could lead to a satisfactory resolution of the Manchurian issue. It does not hesitate to abandon the covenant on which it is based and disregard the facts it has recognized, making contradictory statements to appease the powerful. Regarding the responsibility for the September 18th Incident, it is already known that the Japanese side had a detailed plan prepared, and China did not attack Japanese troops or harm Japanese residents. The Japanese military actions cannot be regarded as a legitimate means of self-defense. Then Japan is clearly the leader in destroying the League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty, and should be subject to appropriate sanctions. Unless the League of Nations resolutions are followed to restore the situation before September 18th, there can be no solution. However, it is said that restoring the old situation is not a solution, abandoning the entire theory of the case and taking into account the illegally created situation. Regarding the reform of the Northeast's politics, it is already known that the three northeastern provinces are entirely Chinese territory, and in no way, legally or factually, can they be separated. Then the improvement of the politics of the three northeastern provinces falls within the scope of China's internal affairs. The Chinese government has its own consistent domestic policy, which should not be subject to foreign interference. However, it is advocated that under the Advisory Council, a special system of government should be organized, and a special gendarmerie should be used to maintain internal security. The appointment of administrative chiefs of the three northeastern provinces, the allocation of taxes, and the central government of China should have no say in them. The special gendarmerie must be trained by foreigners, the tax authorities must be supervised by foreigners, and the central bank of the three northeastern provinces must have a foreigner as the chief advisor. The autonomous government must also hire a considerable number of foreign advisors, with the Japanese occupying an important proportion. In the current situation, the so-called organization of the Advisory Council must also be manipulated by the Japanese. In this way, it is beautifully called autonomy, which is no different from international co-management by Japan. It still says that it maintains China's sovereignty, independence, and territorial integrity. Who will it deceive? The report states that the establishment of new treaty relations between China and Japan, for Japan, advocates that it should freely participate in economic development, promote the rights and interests of residence and land lease, and expand the scope of consular jurisdiction, even including Jehol, which has not yet been occupied by Japan. For China, it advocates that Manchuria should gradually become a demilitarized zone, stipulated by treaty that the demilitarized zone should not be violated, and promise in the commercial treaty to prohibit the domestic boycott of Japanese goods. The League of Nations Covenant, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty cannot stop Japan's aggression, then the so-called non-violation of the demilitarized zone only prevents China from stationing troops for defense. Buying and selling goods is purely a matter of the people's livelihood and cannot be interfered with by the government. Even if there is a boycott movement, there are many examples of peaceful resistance to violence in various countries. How can there be a reason to bear the obligation to prohibit it in the treaty? In the past, the twenty-one demands made by Japan to us, the special rights regarding Manchuria and Mongolia requested were not as harsh as those listed by this investigation team. In this way, it is said to be suitable for the interests of both China and Japan, which is even more ridiculous. As for saying that the solution to the Manchurian problem must consider the interests of the third party, the Soviet Union, it is not known what its significance is. Before Japan conveniently occupied the Northeast, how could China have harmed the interests of the Soviet Union? If the recommendation of the investigation team is followed, maintaining Japan's special power in the Northeast, causing this problem to be unresolved and expanding, will become one of the entire Pacific problems, not just a problem between Japan and the so-called third party. The report also said that the ultimate requirement for appropriate political measures should be, as advocated by Dr. Sun Yat-sen, international cooperation to complete China's internal rejuvenation. It is not known that Premier Sun advocated international joint investment to develop China's industry, which is not the ultimate requirement for appropriate political measures. The development of industry must be under our control, and others cannot take over the responsibility on our behalf. If this is used as a cover for advocating international co-management of the Northeast, it not only misunderstands Premier Sun's teachings, but also clearly contradicts nationalism. In summary, the observation of the report on the facts of Japan's invasion of China is not unclear, and it has made this compromising suggestion, not daring to make a fair proposition. We see here more clearly that the so-called League of Nations and the so-called covenant are really not to be relied upon. The Northeast problem can only be resolved by relying on the strength of our nation. The integrity of China's territory and the independence of sovereignty can also only be maintained by relying on the strength of our nation. From now on, we must bear a firm will and the spirit of sacrifice to continue resistance and seek the recovery of lost territory. The situation is urgent, and there is no room for hesitation. We hope that our government and people will rise up together to plan for it. The Southwest Executive Department of the Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and the Southwest Political Affairs Committee of the National Government respectfully announce, (11th Press Dispatch).

Foreign Affairs Committee Seeks Opinions from All Parties on the Report 25

Luo Wengan Will Visit Chiang Kai-shek in Hankou Today

The Nanjing Foreign Affairs Committee has consulted several times on its opinions on the report, but because it is of great importance, opinions from all parties should be widely solicited, especially the opinions of Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek, which are even more important. However, Wang and Chiang have just read the full text and are still studying it in detail and have not yet expressed their views. Foreign Minister Luo has specifically scheduled to fly to Hankou on the morning of the 14th to meet with Chiang Kai-shek for consultation, return to Nanjing on the 15th, and fly to Shanghai on the 16th to meet with Wang Jingwei for consultation, so that a concrete decision can be made (13th Central Telegram).

A Nanjing reporter met with a government official on the 13th and asked about the extent of the government's discussion of the report of the Investigation Team. According to the official, the government is still seriously discussing this and has not yet made a concrete decision. Currently, there are already many criticisms from various parties about the report, some saying that certain articles and points are still fair, and some saying that certain chapters and sections are absolutely unacceptable. In fact, the discussion and research of such chapters and articles are not where our current energy should be focused. What we should pay the most attention to today is the international atmosphere and the attitude of the Japanese side. The report of the Investigation Team is only a report to the League of Nations. The solution to the Sino-Japanese problem will still be discussed by the General Assembly of the League of Nations. If the Japanese side can change its always stubborn attitude and seek an appropriate solution to the Sino-Japanese problem under the supervision of the League of Nations, then we should start from the big picture and consider a solution based on the principle of not losing rights or humiliating the country. If the Japanese side is still strong, barbarous, and disregards everything, then we should make proper preparations on the one hand, and pay attention to the international situation and the changes arising therefrom at any time. If the international situation deteriorates as a result, then we should make proper plans for all preparations at this time (13th Central News Agency Telegram).

Beiping Luo Wengan telegraphically invites Chiang Menglin and Zhou Zuomin to go to Beijing and convene experts from various places to begin studying the League of Nations report (13th Press Dispatch).

Wife of British Businessman Murdered by Bandits 66

According to foreign dispatches from Beiping, the wife of Mr. Huthruff, an accountant at the British American Tobacco Company in Harbin, was brutally murdered by bandits. Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, Mrs. Huthruff was taking her children to school by car when, not far from their home, they were stopped by three armed bandits who attempted to kidnap her for ransom. Mrs. Huthruff strongly resisted and was shot dead. Her Russian chauffeur was also wounded by a bullet, but his injuries were not serious. Fortunately, none of the children were harmed. After a pursuit, one of the perpetrators was killed and another captured, while one remains at large. (Reuters, 13th)

London: News of the murder of Mrs. Huthruff in Harbin has caused shock here. All newspapers have published the story in large print. The entire family is grief-stricken. (Reuters, 13th)

Beiping: Further details received from Harbin regarding the murder of Mrs. Huthruff indicate that the bandits not only intended to kidnap Mrs. Huthruff but also her children. Two Russians bravely attempted to capture the bandits, who fled. The Russians gave chase, and the bandits fired their weapons as they ran. Both Russians were hit and seriously wounded. Subsequently, Chinese police joined the pursuit and engaged in a gun battle with the bandits. Previous reports stated there were three bandits; it is now known there were four. Two were killed by Chinese police, and two escaped. It is reported that Mrs. Huthruff resisted the bandits in an attempt to protect her children and was murdered as a result. Her children witnessed the entire event. (Reuters, 13th)

Using both bribery and force to deal with the Volunteer Armies.

According to investigations, the so-called new policies are as follows: (1) Regarding the Rehe problem, both bribery and military offensive policies will be used. The methods and timing will be left to the discretion of Commander Mutō. (2) Regarding countermeasures against the Volunteer Armies, the primary emphasis will be on bribery, with military force used only as a last resort. It is best to avoid Japanese casualties. (3) Regarding countermeasures against Su Bingwen's anti-Japanese resistance, consideration must be given to the relationship with Russia, and the rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway and Russian expatriate property must be respected to avoid a direct conflict between Russia and Japan. It is best to invite Russian officers to observe and monitor the fighting. Other issues, such as countermeasures against the Lytton Report and the proposed Russo-Japanese-Manchukuo non-aggression treaty, will also be explained to the Kwantung Army, and the Kwantung Army's opinions will be sought. Major General Nagata's trip is to facilitate communication between the military headquarters and the Kwantung Army, convey military orders, and his mission is of great importance.

Japan Changes Policy Towards the League of Nations 80

Decides to Participate in the Vote

▲ China United News Agency (13th, Tokyo): Recently, there has been a faction within the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs advocating a showdown with the League of Nations, abandoning the previous policy of passive resistance. They argue that the attitude taken by Foreign Ministers Shidehara and Yoshizawa towards the League of Nations—namely, denying the League of Nations' authority to resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute under Article 15 of the League Covenant and participating in the Assembly only as an observer without participating in the vote—should be abandoned. Japan has made a final decision to rescind its previous policy, formally recognize the Assembly's authority under Article 15 of the Covenant, participate in the vote, and demonstrate Japan's resolve. It is said that Foreign Minister Uchida also agrees. If realized, this would be a change in Japan's foreign policy over the past year.

▲ Japan Alliance News (13th, Tokyo): The Seiyukai party has decided to send former Diet member Futami Jinxiang to Geneva to attend the League of Nations Assembly. ▲ Japan Professional News (13th, Tokyo): Representative Ding Nishiyuan of the Trans-Siberian Delegation met with various dignitaries in Tokyo to exchange views. He is scheduled to leave Tokyo for Koga tomorrow, traveling to Geneva via Siberia.

Three Provinces Discuss the Contents of the Memorandum 81

▲ Den-tsu (13th, Tokyo): The three ministries of Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy held a joint meeting this afternoon to finalize the memorandum regarding... and will begin drafting it immediately. It is reported that the memorandum will be approximately 40 pages long and will be completed by the 20th.

▲ China United News Agency (13th, Tokyo): Today, the three ministries of Army, Navy, and Foreign Affairs held a joint meeting to decide on the outline of the Japanese government's memorandum on the Lytton Report. The main points are: (1) The Lytton Report's sources and perspective are unfair. (2) Resolving the Sino-Japanese issue, especially the Manchurian issue, through peaceful means is unrealistic. Based on this position, the memorandum will be drafted under the following six points: (1) Manchuria is historically separate from mainland China and cannot be considered China's original territory. (2) Japan cannot absolutely admit that the September 18th Incident was a planned act by Japan. (3) Japan cannot agree with the view that the establishment of Manchukuo was a Japanese scheme and insists that it represents the will of 30 million Manchurians. (4) China cannot be considered an organized independent state. (5) The responsibility for boycotting Japanese goods lies with China, not with Japan's policy of aggression. (6) China, as a non-organized state, naturally cannot claim territorial integrity or sovereignty.

▲ The Tokyo Yorozu Shimbun reports that the Lytton Commission's disregard for the fact of "Manchukuo's" independence has aroused great indignation among the Japanese people. In particular, Army Minister Araki is outraged by the source of the following material in Section 1 of Chapter 6 of the report: "The independence of Manchuria is related to Japan's new political movement. Japanese civil and military officials, whether in office or not, planned, organized, and implemented this independence movement in terms of solutions to the Manchurian Incident." This material originated after the autumn of last year when middle-ranking officers in the military became dissatisfied with various national policies. At the same time, business circles felt great fear. Therefore, when the commission arrived, these business leaders, solely pursuing the interests of businessmen, provided the commission with malicious material attacking the military, which the commission then used as material for its report. Thus, the reason why the report is unfavorable to Japan is this. The heads of the military and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs now recognize that the business leaders committed this imprudent and traitorous act. It is now clear in the report and they are quite resentful. A major domestic problem is about to erupt.

Foreign Important Telegrams II

Excerpts of the Ottawa Agreement Published 87

British Goods Enjoy Special Preferences

Greatest Impact on Trade Between US and Germany

▲ Reuters (12th, London): Excerpts from the records of the Ottawa British Imperial Economic Conference were published today. The agreement between Britain and Canada stipulates that British goods imported into Canada will have a 40% tax reduction, while Canadian products will be imported into Britain tax-free, limited to a value of 8 million yuan per year. Britain has agreed to impose effective and gradual restrictions on the import of foreign wheat. At present, Britain imports a large quantity of wheat from Argentina. The South American agreement with Britain stipulates that British goods can be imported tax-free, while special taxes will be levied on foreign goods imported into South America. The British-Indian agreement stipulates that 163 types of British goods will enjoy preferential treatment with a 1/10 tax reduction. In the future, cotton and silk goods may also be included in this preferential treatment. Australia will allow a 15-20% tax reduction for British goods. New Zealand will also reduce import taxes on British goods. Britain has promised that certain products from Newfoundland will enjoy a 1/10 tax reduction. The results obtained by the British colonies at the Canadian conference are to increase the provisions for preferential treatment, but the preferential treatment is limited to automobiles from the Straits Settlements and Hong Kong. Malaya benefits from a tax reduction on canned jackfruit. Tropical products, including West Indian fruits and West African vegetable oils, will all enjoy preferential tariffs in the self-governing territories. The above agreements are the results of the Ottawa Imperial Conference.

▲ Kuo Min News Agency (12th, London): Today, the British government published excerpts from the agreements of the Ottawa Imperial Conference. According to the contents, the preferential tariff rates for the British Empire's territories can enable British manufacturers to seize 31 million pounds of trade from foreign merchants. This trade is currently mostly enjoyed by German and American merchants. Therefore, the results of the Ottawa Conference have the greatest impact on the US and Germany. This excerpt is 95 pages long and discloses all the points that have been kept secret so far in the agreements. According to British officials, the value of goods imported by the self-governing territories last year that should be subject to preferential tariff treatment according to the agreement is at least 70 million pounds, with manufactured goods accounting for the majority. The United States has a large amount of these goods sold to Canada and Australia, and this will be greatly affected in the future. The extent to which US exports to the British self-governing territories will be affected has not yet been estimated, but US exports are mostly to Canada. In 1930, US exports of 13 major products to Canada were worth US$34.2 million, mainly coal, iron, and industrial machinery. In the British-Indian agreement made at the Ottawa Conference, it is stipulated that Britain will levy a tax of 1 penny per pound on foreign rice, but not on broken rice.

▲ Havas (12th, Asuncion, Paraguay): It seems that the Paraguayan army has occupied the fortresses of Alihuatá and Garay Castillo. The Bolivian National Army has fled with their weapons one by one.

Unemployed are Instigated by Communists

Continued Transgressions Occur

▲ Reuters (12th, Dublin): The capital of Northern Ireland is more peaceful today, but it is still an armed peace. Important News

Northern Manchuria Under the Iron Heel of the Japanese Army 95

▲ Japanese Army Builds Large Power Grid in Harbin

▲ Mr. and Mrs. Xie Ke Cleverly Deceive the Japanese

▲ Two Major Purposes of the Japanese Army's Designs on Jehol

▲ Peiping Correspondence: Yesterday afternoon, our reporter visited Mr. Xi, a friend who recently arrived in Peiping from Harbin, and inquired about important news from the Northeast. According to him:

▲ Harbin's Economy on the Verge of Bankruptcy: Under the strict maintenance of order by the Japanese puppet military police, robbery cases are increasing daily in Harbin's streets. After 7:00 PM, the more secluded streets are devoid of pedestrians. In the area south of Xiangfang for dozens of li and near Songpu Town north of the river, there are frequent skirmishes between the volunteer army and the Japanese army. In Harbin's streets, the sound of cannons can be heard daily. To prepare for any eventuality, the Japanese army has spent a huge amount of money to build a large power grid around Harbin. On the road from Xiangfang to Harbin (about fifteen li long), the Japanese army has set up multiple checkpoints, where they frequently search pedestrians, especially strictly before 8:00 AM and after 7:00 PM, which effectively cuts off pedestrian traffic. As for Harbin's economic situation, it is virtually on the verge of bankruptcy.

▲ Ma's Army Advances Towards Suihua: Regarding Ma Zhanshan's troops, in addition to a portion actively operating on the Qiqihar line, forming a liaison with Su Bingwen, who has newly raised the banner of resistance, the majority are still actively engaged in sabotage work in the Hulan-Hailun line area. Bridges and railway tracks are frequently destroyed, causing the Hulan-Hailun Railway to operate intermittently. At the end of September, Ma's Zou Regiment and Tian Regiment, etc., fiercely fought the Japanese army for five or six hours at Keyinhe Station, forty li south of Hailun, killing more than thirty Japanese officers and soldiers, and destroying bridges and railway tracks in the vicinity of the station. As of the fifth of this month, when he left Harbin, he heard that Ma's army was taking advantage of the victory and advancing towards Suihua. Due to flooding, Japanese tanks and airplanes were largely ineffective, which was the main reason for the Volunteer Army's victory at that time.

▲ Xie Ke Escapes the Tiger's Mouth: After the Japanese army experienced various difficulties in their operations in northern Dong Province, they decided not to attack militarily unless absolutely necessary. Instead, they adopted a policy of appeasement towards the leaders of the Volunteer Army. Xie Ke, Ma Zhanshan's chief of staff who was previously arrested, was imprisoned in Changchun and later moved to Jiang Province. The Japanese army used various means to persuade Xie to repent and join the puppet state. Xie feigned compliance and submitted a letter of repentance, so the Japanese changed his imprisonment to surveillance. When the Hailun-Manchurian Railway troops revolted, the Japanese army immediately understood Su Bingwen's motives and tried to persuade Su's staff. Mrs. Xie Ke, knowing the intention of the Japanese authorities, seized the opportunity to argue that Xie's visit would be effective, and said that she and Mrs. Su were close friends and were willing to go with Xie. Hayashi Hideichi, the head of the Japanese special service agency, strongly advocated a policy of appeasement, so he agreed to Xie and his wife going to Hailar. After Xie arrived in Hailar, he and Su made large-scale anti-Japanese plans. On the other hand, the arrest warrants for important anti-Japanese figures who had been previously ordered to be arrested were also mostly canceled, and they were allowed to surrender voluntarily. For the more important figures, special personnel were sent to persuade them. It is unknown whether the Japanese will change their persuasion policy after being deceived by Xie's plan.

▲ Japan Further Creates a Mongolian State: From various related sources, we have obtained an even more astonishing piece of news: that the Japanese army is not only creating a "Manchukuo" but also intending to create a Mongolian state. This plan began this spring. However, the Japanese army does not want to adopt an overt military policy, so they first sent many people to various parts of Mongolia to conduct activities. Once the conditions are ripe, they will simultaneously adopt military force. Before completing this plan, the Japanese army in Jehol and the border areas has planned to first take Kailu and Xifeng. Recently, the Japanese army has been actively reinforcing its troops on the Jehol border, partly to threaten Peiping and Tianjin and block traffic to and from the Northeast, and partly to complete this plan. (October 11th)

A Page in the War History of Wang Delin 96

▲ Heroes of Laoye Ridge Achieve Merit

▲ Enemy Ambushed at Hama Pond

A visitor from Kirin in Peiping talked about Wang Delin's National Salvation Army. Since the Japanese army invaded the Northeast, Wang Delin's troops, with the strength of a battalion commander, have risen up to save the country. It has been a year since then, with more than a hundred battles fought, especially the battles of Jingpo Lake and Laoye Ridge being the most fierce. They are recorded separately as follows:

▲ The Battle of Jingpo Lake: Jingpo Lake is located south of Ning'an and east of Laoye Ridge, and is the only way for the National Salvation Army to attack Dunhua. After the Japanese army suffered a defeat in the South Lake Head battle, they led more than a thousand men to counterattack, engaging the National Salvation Army in the area. After two days and nights of fierce fighting, the Japanese army suffered more than three hundred casualties. The remaining troops were surrounded by Wang's army in Jingpo Lake. Three days later, the Japanese army was completely annihilated due to lack of food and ammunition. The guns and artillery were completely captured by the National Salvation Army. After hearing the news, the Japanese army headquarters immediately sent a battalion of guards, a battalion of mortars, three companies of machine guns, and more than ten airplanes for cover, rushing to the rescue. Wang's army, outnumbered, retreated to the vicinity of Dashifeng in South Lake Head and ambushed in the surrounding forests. The Japanese army was unfamiliar with the terrain and came to attack. The National Salvation Army's ambush troops rose up from all sides, annihilating countless enemies and shooting down one airplane, capturing three mortars and five machine guns. The National Salvation Army also suffered more than thirty casualties.

▲ Fierce Battle of Laoye Ridge: A few days after the National Salvation Army's victory at Jingpo Lake, they recovered Ning'an and continued to occupy Hailin, Mudanjiang, and Hengdaohezi. The National Salvation Army then set out in three routes: Kong Xianrong's troops advanced along the Chinese Eastern Railway to attack Yimianpo, Wu Yicheng's troops advanced straight to Dunhua along Jingpo Lake, and Wang Yichen's brigade crossed Daqingbei Mountain to attack Hunchun. After more than ten days of fierce fighting, they successively occupied Yimianpo and Dunhua, but failed to capture Hunchun. After Wang's troops entered Dunhua, they immediately seized Laoye Ridge, the most important and dangerous point for attacking Kirin Province. The Japanese army, in order to rescue Kirin, dispatched a large force from Yanji and launched the first attack on Laoye Ridge and Hama Pond. Only a dozen sentries of the National Salvation Army defended the enemy in dangerous places. For a time, the sound of guns and cannons shook the mountains. Our reinforcements rushed to the scene and switched to the offensive. After more than two hours of fierce fighting, the Japanese army retreated due to the rugged mountain paths and complex forests. Our army did not pursue them. Three days later, the Japanese army launched a second attack on Laoye Ridge from Yanji.

▲ Annihilating the Japanese Army at Night: The Japanese army passed through Xiaochengzi and, as it was already dusk, camped there. This was detected by Ma, the battalion commander of the National Salvation Army, who led his troops to attack while the Japanese army was asleep. That night, the sky was extremely dark, and it was difficult to distinguish faces. When the National Salvation Army arrived at Xiaochengzi, it was almost three o'clock in the morning. They immediately charged into the Japanese army camp, all using bayonets to stab and kill. The Japanese army was caught in their sleep and suffered more than two hundred casualties. The rest fled in panic, and the guns, ammunition, and horses were all captured by Battalion Commander Ma. Three days later, after two defeats, the Japanese army dispatched a large force from Yanji, covered by airplanes, and launched a third attack on Laoye Ridge. Because the Japanese army was coming on strong, the National Salvation Army laid ambushes in various parts of the ridge and ordered that the key point of Hama Pond be abandoned. When the Japanese army approached Laoye Ridge, they ordered an encirclement from all sides. After a day and night of mixed warfare, the Japanese army began to retreat due to heavy casualties. However, because the key point of Hama Pond was still captured by the National Salvation Army, they could not withdraw and were in complete disarray. Only more than two hundred people escaped. In this battle, a total of more than 1,200 enemies were annihilated, more than 300 were wounded, and many small cannons and rifles were captured. The National Salvation Army also suffered nearly a hundred casualties.

New Trends in the Resolution of the Shandong Crisis 97

▲ Jiang Bocheng Talks About Resolution Within a Week

▲ Satisfactory Results from Li and Fan's Negotiations with Liu's Representatives

Jinan Correspondence: Li Yue and Fan Yuhuang, the investigators sent by the Ministry of Military Affairs to investigate the Shandong crisis, are currently inspecting in Shahe and meeting with representatives of Liu Zhennian. The results of their inspections and meetings are being reported to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek daily. After completing their mission, they will return to Jinan soon. According to reports here, Liu Zhennian's troops must eventually be transferred out of Shandong and withdraw from Yexian within a recent period, concentrating within the area designated by the Central Government. It is now waiting for Liu Zhennian's expression to realize this. Today, our reporter visited Jiang Bocheng, who is responsible for handling this matter in Jinan on behalf of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and inquired about everything. According to him, he came to Jinan to discuss with Chairman Han Fuju according to the meaning of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Chairman Han complies with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's opinions in every way. The follow-up solution has been roughly determined, and the follow-up problem can be completely solved within a week at most. It has not yet reached the time for publication. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent a telegram expressing his sympathy for Han's magnanimity and absolute obedience. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek also sent a telegram to Li, the advisor sent by the Ministry of Military Affairs, instructing him to enter Yexian City to discuss with Liu Zhennian (because the radio in Yexian cannot communicate with Nanjing). It is reported that Li has arranged to meet Liu's representatives at Shili Pu in Yexian. It is not certain whether he will meet Liu.

Song Shiyan, the director of the Peiping office of Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuju, received a telegram from Han and took the Peiping-Pukou train from Peiping to Jinan early on the 11th. According to Song at the station, the situation in the Jiaodong incident is very good in all aspects. Director Zhang Xueliang's expression is especially good. He once said that this incident must be completely resolved by transferring Liu Zhennian's troops out of Shandong in the end. About the chief advisor Chiang (Bocheng) returning to Peiping, there will always be a solution. I (Song himself) came here this time at the request of Chairman Han, and there will be no long delay. I will return to Peiping in a few days.

Regarding the situation of the negotiations between the investigators of the Ministry of Military Affairs, Li and Fan, and Liu Zhennian's side in Yexian, according to a Shahe telegram on the 12th, Li Yue and Fan Yuhuang went to Shili Pu at 10:00 AM on the 11th to wait for Liu Zhennian's representative, Li Weihua. At about 12:00 PM, Li was led out of the city by a scholar. The provincial side first sent people to wait at the defense line. After Li arrived, they went to Shili Pu together. The houses were inconvenient, so they changed to an empty room in a temple to meet and talk secretly. The content of the conversation was extremely secret. After about an hour, they finished talking and were escorted out of the defense area and returned to the city by the provincial side. Li Yue said after returning to Shahe at 3:00 PM that the result was very satisfactory. He guaranteed that he would no longer shoot and would absolutely stop military actions, waiting for the central government to deal with it. I will inspect the city, but I must wait for Li to return to the city and ask Liu for instructions before determining when (the 13th) to go out of the city again to discuss.

As for the tragic situation of the siege of Laiyang, according to a Shahe telegram on the 12th: (1) Ge Zhaozeng, the secretary of the Laiyang Party Committee, Wang Baozhen, the principal of the Fourth Elementary School, Zhou Laibao, and the representatives of the gentry and merchants, Li Shaobai, Ge Ziyou, and Zhang Rulin, came to Shahe on the 11th on behalf of all the people of Laiyang to visit the central investigators, requesting the central government to hold the principle of pacifying people and peacefully resolving the Shandong matter. According to reports, there are a total of six regiments of Liu's army in Laiyang. In addition to the 456th Regiment of Liang Ligui's Brigade, there are a stationed regiment, a special service regiment, and a training regiment. Deputy Division Commander He Yisan lives in the county government and presides over everything. Actively build defensive fortifications. The moats are dug in the suburbs, and there are gun holes around the city. Soldiers move without going through the streets. They pass through by digging through the walls of civilian houses. Therefore, no soldiers can be seen on the main streets. Holes are dug everywhere. All departments work underground. Traffic outside the city is all through underground tunnels, without going through the city gates. The first line of defense is at Mashan Fort in the west of the city, using the mountains as a defense. Within twenty miles along the city, people and animals are extinct. All edible food, rice, cattle, and horses are looted and transported to the city for long-term resistance. It is still intended to transfer through Yexian. The people in the city have no freedom of movement. All those who go in and out are those who purchase supplies for the army, but they also need to have a license because they are afraid of leaking the situation in the city. The two armies are still twenty or thirty miles apart. The new county magistrate, Yang Yougui, and the head of the public security bureau, Dou Yaogeng, have set up an administrative office in Shuigoutou, fifty miles southwest of the city. The brigade headquarters is also in Shui. (December 12th)

Liu Wenjin, the Main Culprit in the Embezzlement of Dike Funds, Sentenced to Death 99

▲ Chiang Kai-shek Orders Military Law to be Applied

Hankou Correspondence: Liu Wenjin, the accountant of the Hubei Dike Construction Fund Management Committee, colluded with Cha Wenchü, the manager of the Sichuan Jianglong Opium Company, to embezzle dike funds to the tune of hundreds of thousands of yuan. Recently, the Wuchang District Court sentenced Liu to five years of imprisonment. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek believed that Liu's intentions were malicious and the sentence was too light. He specially submitted it to the Military Law Department, which sentenced him to death in accordance with military law. On the 12th, the criminal Liu was taken to the vicinity of Xinyang Restaurant on Liudu Bridge, Minquan Road, and executed by shooting. The charges are recorded as follows: "Re: Announcing the charges. Liu Wenjin, the accountant of the Hubei Provincial Dike Construction Fund Management Committee, colluded with Cha Wenchü, the manager of the Sichuan Jianglong Company, to embezzle a huge amount of money. The case was first tried by the Wuchang District Court and sentenced to five years of imprisonment, but the dereliction of duty was not penalized. This headquarters believes that the punishment is too light and is not enough to deter corruption. Liu Wenjin was submitted to the Military Law Department for interrogation. After investigation, the criminal's intentions were malicious, seeking personal gain, and disregarding the lives of the people of the province. How can such a crime be concluded with only five years of imprisonment? He should be shot immediately in accordance with military law to deter corruption and clarify the law. In addition to binding the criminal Liu Wenjin to the execution ground for execution by shooting, this is a special announcement to let everyone know." The announcement included: "Liu Wenjin, 33 years old, from Changsha, Hunan." (November 12th)

Songjiang 100

▲ Another Female Philanthropist Passes Away: Madam Fei, the stepmother of Zheng Bocang of this county, who is over seventy years old, is kind and benevolent and likes to do good. She has sponsored many local charitable and public welfare undertakings. The General Office of the Chinese Red Cross Society in Shanghai once specially presented her with a plaque of pine and longevity to commend her. This time, the Songjiang Red Cross Branch plans to raise funds to establish a charitable hospital to benefit the sick. Madam Fei once again made a grand wish, instructing her wise son Zheng Bocang to sponsor the plan and wishing to make the first donation to show her advocacy. Unexpectedly, after autumn, Madam Fei contracted a minor illness. Without seeing its completion, she passed away on the eleventh of this month. Those who heard about it regretted it. The funeral was held yesterday, with plain cars and white horses, and mourners, which was very grand for both life and death.

Suzhou 101

▲ Building a National Soul Tomb at Tiger Hill: The officers and soldiers of the First Regiment of the Garrison Military Police, many of whom died during the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai, were initiated by the former regiment leader Jin Deyang to build a National Soul Tomb on the open space in front of Zhishuang Pavilion in Tiger Hill, burying the remains of the fallen officers and soldiers in a scenic spot to comfort the loyal souls and provide a memorial. Later, Regiment Leader Jin was ordered to be transferred to the Jiangxi Eighteenth Army Cadre Training Corps as the captain of the officer corps. He felt it was inappropriate to suspend the National Soul Tomb matter, so he sent a letter to Shi Kuihe, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, asking him to handle it on his behalf. After receiving the letter, Shi is now planning everything and will start work soon. From then on, the scenic spot of Tiger Hill will have another kind of memorial for people to mourn.

▲ Auctioning Enemy Coal to Help the Volunteer Army: The Anti-Japanese Association of this county recently seized sixty-five tons of Japanese coal from the Shenhe Coal Shop outside Xumen Huangting Street. The Standing Committee ruled that it should be confiscated and auctioned, and the proceeds would be handed over to the Chamber of Commerce for donating to the Northeast Volunteer Army. It is now learned that the enemy coal has been purchased by the Xinfu Rock and Coal Company for six taels of silver per ton, totaling 390 taels.

Wuxi 102

▲ Ancient Tomb of the Ming Dynasty Discovered at General Bridge: Under the General Bridge inside the East Gate of this county, on the west side of the Furen Middle School, there is an open space, which is the private property of the Ao family and rented to Furen as a playground. Yesterday, the school hired workers to level the playground. In the center of the playground, they suddenly dug up a square green stone about two or three feet in size. The words "Tomb of Ming Scholar Gengyun Chen Jun" are engraved on the stone. The script is ancient. When the Ao family heard about it, they instructed the workers to continue digging. Before they dug down two feet, they dug up another green stone of the same size. Because it had been buried in the soil for four or five hundred years, the writing was blurred and difficult to distinguish, even after the workers washed it repeatedly. It was only known that it was the date of birth and death and the life history of the person in the tomb. According to the records, the era should be the third dynasty of the Ming Dynasty, the time of Emperor Chengzu. Stone mines were also found under the stone, with two coffins inside, both of which were rotten. Only two sets of bones remained, with particularly large skulls, and dozens of ancient coins and several toys were buried. Ao then took them home for research.

▲ The Silk Factory Workers' Strike Situation Expands: A strike broke out in 25 silk factories throughout Wuxi County on the 8th. After the party and government authorities earnestly mediated, it was decided that the factories would resume work on the 12th. However, when the factories started work at that time, a few women came out to obstruct it, led by male workers with different lengths of clothing. They first caused trouble in three factories in the northern district, including Dacheng, Dechang, and Huisheng. The glass doors and windows on the outside were all broken. Seeing the fierce momentum, the three factories immediately stopped work, and the female workers were coerced to disperse. The loss reached more than 2,000 yuan. At 10:00 AM, the striking workers went to the Jinji Silk Factory in the western district to force a shutdown. They first made a noise outside the factory, then smashed the glass windows and wooden buckets, and used iron hooks to explore the silk and cut off all the silk that had not been finished. The silk threads on the car were also pulled off. Fortunately, the county police team rushed to the scene after hearing the news and dispersed them. The factory suffered the most damage, estimated at more than 3,000 taels of silver. The affected factories immediately sent letters to the industry association, requesting the county government to demand compensation. In the afternoon, Director He of the Department of Industry believed that if the workers' strike was not resolved as soon as possible, accidents would inevitably occur. In addition to appointing inspector Zhou Juesheng to come to Wuxi to mediate, he also sent Jiang Nanchun, the secretary of the department, to Wuxi in the afternoon to assist in handling the matter. Chen, the county magistrate, gathered the standing committee members of the labor and capital parties, as well as the two provincial committee members Jiang and Zhou, Sun Danchen of the provincial party department, and Xu Yongyi of the county party department to the county to discuss the matter. The capitalists said that if the silk merchants were to fail again, if they were not forgiven by the labor side, they would have to sacrifice with pain and temporarily close down. The labor side said that the workers had simple ideas and persuasion was ineffective, and they could only wait for the members' congress to resolve it. After joint consultation between the party and government, it was decided to convene a mediation meeting of the labor and capital parties at 2:00 PM on the 15th, and notices have been sent. On that day, except for the four factories that were destroyed, the female workers in the remaining factories voluntarily went to the factories to work because they were eager to make a living, and were not affected in any way. As of yesterday (13th), except for the four factories that could not work due to damage, the rest went to work as usual. However, at noon, a small number of female workers from the northern district, led by people who looked like male workers, flocked to the Gansheng Silk Factory and smashed the doors and windows. Fearing that the strike would expand again, the capitalists believed that the strike was a local problem from beginning to end. If the government had no definite way to deal with those who instigated strikes and gathered crowds to riot, the factories would rather sacrifice and would not accept any oppressive conditions.

Furthermore, according to a long-distance telephone message, the Gansheng Silk Factory suddenly started work at about 1:00 PM yesterday because it did not fulfill the conditions. When the nearby female workers heard the news, they immediately gathered four or five hundred people and flocked to the factory to accuse them. The momentum was fierce. The Public Security Bureau sent a large number of police officers to the scene to suppress them and persuade the female workers, but to no avail. They fired several empty shots, and the female workers dispersed. At that time, more than a dozen female workers were injured in the head, face, and other parts by police officers with sticks. Afterwards, County Magistrate Chen reported the incident to the Department of Civil Affairs by telephone. It is said that the county magistrate and Public Security Bureau Chief Wu will go to the province this morning to ask for instructions. Wu Jianzhou, the chief of the Second Division of the Department of Construction, went to Wuxi to mediate. Jiang Nanchun, the secretary of the Department of Industry, took a car to Zhenjiang after 6:00 PM last night to report the details. The Silk Factory Association advised the factories to continue to suspend work and wait for the party and government agencies to mediate on the 15th to avoid expanding the workers' strike.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Sternly Reprimands Zhenhuan Elementary School for Falsely Claiming Registration 108

(Shanghai News Agency) The Shanghai Private Zhenhuan Elementary School, without being registered, printed the words "Registered by the Municipal Bureau of Education" on its enrollment advertisements and posted them everywhere in an attempt to deceive. After investigation by the Municipal Bureau of Education, a reprimand order has been issued. The text of the order is as follows: "Upon investigation, this Bureau has found that the said school has not been approved for registration by this Bureau and has unauthorizedly printed the words 'Registered by this Bureau' on its enrollment advertisements and posted them everywhere. It is confirmed by this Bureau that the said school's false claim of registration should be reprimanded. Furthermore, it is ordered to promptly make corrections."

The Municipal Council's Elementary Schools Will Increase Tuition Fees Starting Next Spring 109

The tuition fees for the Municipal Council's Chinese elementary schools are quite low. Recently, the director of the Chinese Education Department investigated the economic circumstances of the students' families and suggested that the tuition fees be appropriately increased. During the discussion of this matter at the last Education Committee meeting, the deputy director of finance stated that the curriculum of these schools seemed to be higher than originally proposed, and therefore the fees should be slightly closer to those of middle schools. The director of the Chinese Education Department then stated that the curriculum of these elementary schools was fundamental to education, but that the higher grades had subjects slightly akin to those of middle schools. Subsequently, a committee member stated that the facilities of each school were relatively complete, and the expenses were also considerable, so the tuition fees should naturally be increased. The chairman replied that the tuition fees for public schools should naturally be lower. Currently, there are many students in the schools who can afford higher tuition fees, but it is difficult to refuse their admission. At the same time, another committee member stated that the parents of the students, in their capacity as taxpayers, already bear a portion of the school's expenses. After discussion, it was decided that, starting next spring, (1) the tuition fees for Eastern District Elementary School and Huade Road Elementary School will be increased from three yuan to six yuan per semester, and (2) the tuition fees for Western District Elementary School and Northern District Elementary School will be increased from three yuan to eight yuan per semester. Each school may admit free students, up to one-tenth of the student body, to help poor children. This proposal has already been adopted and implemented by the Municipal Council's Board of Directors at its meeting this past Wednesday.

In the past few days, each athlete must pay attention to the following items: (1) Decline all social engagements; (2) Do not participate in other sports, causing unexpected events such as ankle injuries; (3) Abstain from eating indigestible and unclean fruits; (4) Pay extra attention to clothing and sleep. Tomorrow is the opening ceremony of the conference. All athletes are permitted to go to the Chinese basketball luncheon at 11:30 AM, hold a meeting at 12:00 PM to elect the team captain, distribute number cloths and sports clothing, and take a group photo.

▲ The News Will Be Broadcast by Youlian Radio Station: The current National Games will be held on the 15th and 16th of this month. The winners and losers are of great interest to people of all countries. Youlian Company Broadcasting Radio Station, located at 241 Avenue Joffre, is very concerned about international sports news. It has now reached an agreement with the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation. At that time, personnel will be sent to the venue to record the results of various preliminary and final competitions, and the results will be reported on the radio station throughout the day. Those who have installed wireless radio receivers are requested to pay attention.

Three National Records for Men's Events at the North China Games 117

▲Triple jump... 13.94 meters

▲Shot put... 12.24 meters

▲Javelin throw... 47.26 meters

Kaifeng, 12th: The 16th North China Games saw the creation of three new national records in the senior and intermediate men's categories. (1) Situ Guangzhi's triple jump of 13.94 meters; (2) Liu Renxiu's 16-pound shot put of 12.24 meters; both are senior category. (3) In the intermediate category, Bian Zuoyun's javelin throw of 47.26 meters. Zhou Longen's 46.89 meters is also a new national record.

Kaifeng, 12th: The results of the track and field events over two days show that Beiping won the men's senior track championship and the men's intermediate field championship. Hebei won the men's senior field championship and the men's intermediate track championship. Shandong won the women's championship, and Henan was the runner-up.

Kaifeng, 12th: At the annual meeting of the North China Athletic Federation held at the Henan Sports Field on the morning of the 13th, it was decided that the next North China Athletic Federation Congress will be held in Taiyuan, and the soccer and basketball games will be held in Jinan. A Record of a Tennis Performance in Beijing (Part 1) - Sun, Lin, Fang 119

This time, because of the invitation of Mr. Huang Shaoxiong and Mr. Chen Gongbo, we went from Shanghai to Nanjing to hold a fundraising tennis match. The ticket revenue was all remitted to the Northeastern Volunteer Army. Therefore, Daozhang, Zhaojia, Deguang, Baohua, Feihai, along with a reporter, a group of six people, took the night train to Beijing on Friday. Although the performance in Beijing was only for a short two days, there were several situations worth savoring at the time. Now, because of the instructions of friends Qiu, Lin, Zheng, Jiang, and Liang, I am writing them down in a hurry (editor's note: Mr. Sun has already left for Haizhou to take up his post).

We took the 11 o'clock express train that night and arrived in Nanjing at 7:30 the next day. Mr. Feng Jiangang and others were already waiting at the station. After meeting, we took a car to Lizhi Society, rested for a while, and Mr. Feng asked for our opinions on whether to take a bath first or eat first. A Jia (Zhaojia)'s stomach had been hungry all night, and without waiting for our reply, he hurriedly said, "Let's eat first." We smiled at each other and walked into the dining hall. A Jia didn't say a word, just lowered his head and devoured his food. In the blink of an eye, four eggs and two plates of ham were swept away without a trace. When he wanted to add more, we said, "A Jia, you still have to play ball this morning." Although A Jia put down his knife and fork, he puffed up his cheeks and glared at us.

Around 10 o'clock, we practiced for a while on the Lizhi Society court. At 2 o'clock in the afternoon, the competition officially started. The temporary order was Deguang vs. the reporter in singles, Baohua and Zhaojia vs. Feihai and Daozhang in doubles, and then Baohua and Deguang vs. the Beijing famous players Ling Daoyang and Ma Qingxi in doubles. The result of the singles match was:

Liang Deguang 7-5, 4-6, Sun Linfang (each winning one set)

Deguang was originally a famous Hong Kong hard court tennis player. The reporter also likes to play on hard courts, so playing on the Lizhi Society hard court was very enjoyable. The result of the first doubles match was:

Zheng Zhaojia and Lin Baohua 8, Jiang Daozhang 6, Qiu Feihai, draw

Lin Zheng's combination in the first set was impeccable. Sometimes, they used small tricks to catch the opponent off guard. At the beginning of the second set, Qiu Jiang suddenly showed great magic, with surprise moves coming out one after another. Therefore, the result of the two dramatic sets was a tie, with a score of one to one. This battle was full of highlights and won a lot of applause. The result of the second doubles match was:

Liang Deguang and Lin Baohua 6-3, Ma Qingxi 6-2, Ling Daoyang, Lin Liang won

Mr. Ling Daoyang is already over forty years old, and he can still tirelessly compete on the court. Indeed, he is getting stronger as he gets older and can serve as a model for future generations. Mr. Ma's tennis skills are also commendable. However, encountering Baohua and Deguang for the first time, he inevitably had to concede slightly.

After the competition, the sky was getting dark. The general manager of Lizhi Society, Mr. Huang Renlin, invited us to dinner. In addition to the six of us, there were also members of the Shanghai Singing Troupe, gathered together, talking and laughing happily. After the banquet, Mr. Feng, Mr. Yu, and Mr. Chen invited us to a tea party at the International Club. There, we met many friends from overseas. We talked about old times endlessly and didn't say goodbye until after 2 o'clock.

When we returned to Lizhi Society, our car left first. We didn't expect that after we arrived, their car was nowhere to be seen. The room assignment was that Baohua and Zhaojia were in the same room, but the key was with Baohua. Baohua had not yet arrived, and Zhaojia was already very sleepy. However, the iron general was guarding the gate, and he could not enter. Zhaojia was as anxious as an ant on a hot pot, bumping into things everywhere. Finally, he couldn't wait any longer and fell asleep on A Liang's bed. We were also too tired, so we were about to fall asleep when suddenly we heard Baohua calling A Jia, A Jia upstairs all the way. After we asked, we learned that the reason they hadn't come for so long was because the car had broken down in a secluded place and had been repaired for a long time before it was driven. Just like A Jia, the two of them were "anxious!" Hahaha.

We slept very well at night, but Taul (Daozhang)'s snoring, like thunder, often made us inexplicably open our eyes and look at him a few times.

New Basketball Techniques (10) (2) (Not for Reprinting) Originally Written by Clairo Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin 120

The team trained by the American basketball coach Francis A. Schmidt is known as the winning army. Every time in the championship, taking the first place is as easy as taking something out of a pocket. He has won five consecutive championships in the Southwest League of Arkansas. His Texas Christian team also won the Group B League Championship in winter. Now, one of his formations is shown below. Number 3 rushes out to receive the ball passed by Number 1 to the side of the free throw area. After passing the ball, Number 1 rushes to the bottom of the basket. At the same time, Number 4 rushes out from the corner to the side of Number 2 to obstruct Number 2's defense. Number 2 then takes the opportunity to rush across the free throw line to receive the pass from Number 3, and then dribbles straight to the basket, or lifts it into the basket from under the basket, or passes it to Number 1 to throw it in.

Financial and Precious Metals Market Stagnation 121

▲Minimal Fluctuations, Slight Decrease of Six Candareens

Yesterday, the precious metals market was dull with minimal fluctuations. The total difference for the day was only 2.4 taels. As a result, the price decreased slightly by six candareens compared to the previous day. The market atmosphere was stagnant, and there were still few transactions. This was because the silver market showed no signs of prosperity or decline. The opening price was extremely flat, followed by slight fluctuations of one or two taels. The foreign exchange market was stable, both official and unofficial rates remaining flat. The future market was even more lackluster, as the impending rollover deterred most parties from showing interest. The price stood around 33 taels. The Central Bank continued to purchase spot goods, totaling approximately 700 bars. Companies like Taikang Run, Tongfeng Heng, Run Changyu sold over 600 bars in the morning session, with prices ranging from 34.8 to 33.5 taels. In the afternoon session, Taikang Run sold another 105 bars at 33.4 taels. It is said that all firms had already offset their November contracts. A detailed record of the entire day is as follows:

▲Morning Market Calm

The market opened with November at 734 taels, the same as the previous day's closing price. Large silver bars for near-term delivery rose slightly by 1/16. Far-term remained unchanged. Due to the holiday, there was no market in the United States, so there were no reports on U.S. cotton. The price then fell from 34.1 to 3.6 taels as Heng Yu, Fu Yu, and others sold off. During this time, Banque Belge sold US$5,625 for January delivery to Socony, and also absorbed US$75 for February. Old Citibank absorbed US$5,625 for January delivery. Additionally, Yifeng Yongheng Changyong and others bought in, pushing the price up by one or two taels. Around 9:30 AM, the price reached 4.6 taels, then leveled off, fluctuating by only a few candareens. At 9:30 AM, HSBC listed exchange rates, with only the German mark increasing by 0.0025, while others remained unchanged. The domestic market was stable. China Bank mutually traded 125 British pounds for October delivery and 1,875 for December delivery. The gold price was 34.5 taels, then shifted to 4.1 taels. As the Central Bank aggressively purchased spot goods, Qian Changxiang (Taikang Run), Tongfeng Heng, and others offset their term positions. Heng Yu, Dade Cheng, and others followed suit. At 10:10 AM, the price was 34.7 taels. Soon after, HSBC released US$3,125 for October delivery, Banque Belge released half-dollar for December. A flurry of selling came from Daxing Yong, Fuyu Hengyu, Yuantai, Tianfeng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, Yifeng Yongfu Tai Xiang, and others, causing a sharp drop of 2 taels. Near 11:00 AM, the price was 32.6 taels. Suddenly, Hengxing and others bought in. Old Citibank also bought US$625 for December delivery. It was rumored that the Central Bank continued to release cash. In just over ten minutes, the price increased to 3.6 taels. Sellers quickly became active, such as Heng Yu, Xiexing Yong, Ri Changchun, Yuan Yongyuan Tai, and others, causing the price to fall again by over one tael. At 11:30 AM, the price settled at 32.3 taels. Later, with Bingxing, Heng Yu, and others buying in, the price increased by one tael to 3.3 taels. Yuan Mao, Chun Yuan Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, and others sold out, so the morning session closed at 32.8 taels.

▲Afternoon Market Uninteresting for All Firms

The afternoon market opened at 32.6 taels. Hengchang Yongyuantai bought in, and Shanghai Banque Belge mutually traded US$4,375 for November delivery, pushing the price up to 33.2 taels. Afterward, Daxing Yong Heng Yu Yuan Mao Yong came out to sell. Citibank sold US$4,375 for November delivery, and Banque Belge sold US$625 for January delivery. At 2:30 PM, the price was 32.4 taels. Daxing Yong Qian Changxiang Dade Cheng bought in, and the Central Bank absorbed cash again, bringing the price to 3.6 taels at 3:00 PM. Heng Yu Zhaofeng Chang sold out, causing a decrease to 2.6 taels. Subsequently, it seemed to rise again. Chase and HSBC mutually traded US$625 for January delivery. Sharp Decline in Foreign Silver Dollars 124

Tianjin Stops Loading...Banks Overbought

Other Ports Still Supplying...Supply Especially Strong

Yesterday, banks had overbought silver dollars, and there was already a weakening trend in the morning. However, due to the recent surge in foreign silver dollar prices, many long positions had profited and were eager to sell. Furthermore, the Tianjin group wired yesterday to stop loading, compounding the difficulties, leading to a major shift in market sentiment. The intensity of the price fluctuations was unprecedented, even during wartime. This shows that while the market may be resilient, public sentiment is still like a startled bird, unable to withstand major storms. From this reporter's perspective, the overall outlook is still good. Although the Tianjin group has stopped loading, other ports continue to supply steadily, offering great hope for market realization.

▲Sharp Decline of Seven Candareens in Foreign Silver Dollars

The morning price of foreign silver dollars was 7.105 candareens, down 0.035 candareens from the previous morning. The afternoon market continued to fall by another 0.035 candareens to 7.07 candareens. This kind of violent decline was evident in the turbulent times. If this kind of movement happened in peaceful times, it would definitely attract attention. (Silver Discount Rate) The morning and afternoon discount rates were both 4%, a rise of 1% from the previous day. The overnight water rate reversed, falling to 7-8%. The silver situation was not very tight.

▲Provincial Silver Coins and Copper Coins Followed the Rise and Fall of Foreign Silver Dollars

In the end, they fell by 0.02 candareens. Trading volume was 14,000 coins in the morning and 5,500 coins in the afternoon. Nantong Cotton Crop Still Good 128

|New Cotton Selling Price Flat and Weak|

A dispatch from Nantong stated that the cotton harvest in the county this year varied greatly by region. Recently, due to unfavorable weather, there was some impact on yield and quality. Based on the current situation, good fields have yielded over 70 catties per mu, while poor fields have yielded only 20 catties. On average, the final result may not differ much from the initial estimate.

(Another dispatch) The Nantong Cotton Industry Association stated that Tong cotton has always been known for its reputation. In recent years, due to farmers adhering to old methods, the production volume has sharply decreased. In addition, ignorant farmers often adulterated cotton with water for profit, resulting in declining quality. In addition to jointly researching and improving seeds with farms, the association issued a notice on the 26th to all ginning shops and farmers within the territory, strictly prohibiting the sale of damp cotton, with violators to be handed over to the authorities for punishment. After the new Nantong cotton came on the market, due to weak market interest, prices remained flat and weak. On the 26th, the price of seed cotton was 16 yuan per shi (approximately 120 lbs), and the price of ginned cotton was 45-46 yuan. Many farmers withheld their goods, waiting for better prices.
