Regulating Rice Prices 143

▲Speech by Minister Soong

Minister of Finance, Soong Tzu-wen, recently, in view of the dumping of foreign rice and the drastic drop in rice prices, which has a significant impact on the rural economy, convened a meeting of representatives from rice-producing provinces, municipalities, and the Ministries of Interior and Industry a few days ago to discuss the regulation of food for the people. It is proposed to use tariff policies to protect the rural economy and regulate rice prices, and to extend this to the circulation of domestic food and the encouragement of stockpiling. It is said that concrete measures have been discussed and the results are very satisfactory. Implementing this plan will benefit both the livelihood of the common people and the rural economy. The details of the meeting have been reported in previous newspapers. We now have access to a speech given by Minister Soong at the meeting, which is disclosed as follows:

Our country is an agricultural nation. According to the ratio of farmland area to population, the rice produced each year should be able to reach a level of self-sufficiency without the need for external sources. However, examining the number of rice imports over the years, there has been an annual increase. Taking only foreign rice as an example, the import volume in the first year of the Republic was 2.7 million dan, which increased to 19.89 million dan in the 19th year of the Republic, a seven-fold increase. Although it decreased somewhat in the 20th year, the import volume from January to June of this year has reached more than 13 million dan, with a value of about 69 million taels of customs silver, which undoubtedly harms the national economy. The cheap sale of foreign rice has caused the selling price of domestic rice to fall below the necessary production cost, which is enough to plunge farmers into despair. At a time when all countries are striving to develop product dumping for their own benefit, we must urgently seek to implement rice policies to alleviate the current difficulties. After detailed consideration of the decline in domestic rice prices, although there are other reasons, the two most significant factors are the prohibition of rice exports from various provinces, preventing free circulation, and the sharp increase in foreign rice imports. The rice-producing provinces often have restrictions on sales, with each province having its own restrictions, and even each county having its own restrictions, which prevents domestic rice from circulating freely within the country, using the method of adjusting surpluses and deficits to maintain the balance of rice prices. This evil system of suppressing the trade of domestic rice further promotes the large-scale import of foreign rice, thus harming both farmers and the people's food supply. It is now proposed to follow the following principles to seek relief: (1) Domestic rice in various provinces should be freely circulated without obstruction. (2) If the price of domestic rice falls to a certain level, a progressive import tax should be imposed on foreign rice. If it exceeds the assumed price, the import tax should be waived. Regarding the first item, the prohibition of rice, the government has long issued clear orders of reprimand, but unfortunately, the provinces have failed to comply uniformly. In the future, when foreign rice is subject to taxation, domestic rice should be even more freely circulated to achieve the practical effect of rescuing agriculture, and there will be no fear of food shortages in areas that do not produce rice. It is hoped that the provinces will earnestly implement this. Regarding the second item, the method of levying import taxes on foreign rice is a flexible tax law. Originally, most countries, except for one or two countries such as Britain and Belgium that must rely on foreign food supply, have implemented taxation on imported rice. In the past, our country was restricted by treaties, which stipulated tax exemption in the tariff regulations. Fortunately, we now have tariff autonomy, and the treaty clauses that have bound China's tax rights have been abolished. Whether to levy or exempt taxes can be freely determined by us. However, there are good and bad harvests every year. If grain is too cheap, it will harm farmers, and if grain is too expensive, it will affect the people's food supply. Therefore, the act of increasing taxes must first conduct a detailed investigation and determination of the standard price of domestic rice in order to take into account both aspects and determine the tax amount, so as to avoid disadvantages. It is hoped that representatives from various provinces will conduct detailed research on the production and sales of rice in their respective provinces. Next, the issue of agricultural loans is also an important plan for rescuing agriculture. The government should immediately find ways to supervise, encourage, and guarantee that banks will do their best to accept the pledge and loans of rice, providing convenience to farmers. Only when agricultural funds can be activated can they maintain the benefits they deserve from their harvest and strive for the development of agriculture. Taking this opportunity of your discussions on this case, I would like to state my views and hope that you will express your great opinions, conduct joint research, and facilitate the promotion of this plan.

Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association Sends a Telegram to the Central Government Requesting Strict Orders to Stop the Sichuan War 144

▲Liu Xiang Reports on the War Situation

The Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai sent an urgent telegram to the government yesterday, stating: "To the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Military Affairs Commission, we have repeatedly received news from Sichuan that the troops of Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui have engaged in actual mixed warfare. Looking ahead, the Sichuan situation is becoming increasingly unimaginable. The feud between the two Lius is not of recent origin. If the government could have acted decisively and rectified discipline, it would not have come to this today. Now, the two Lius are fighting fiercely without any scruples, as if showing the central government. How will the government deal with this matter? Will it still act as a peacemaker as it did in the war between Han and Liu, thus repeating the mistakes of Huan and Ling? The central government will have no credibility. Moreover, although there are many reasons for the warlords in Sichuan daring to engage in mixed warfare, the lack of prestige of the central government and its perfunctory handling of matters are indeed contributing factors. Take Yang Sen as an example, who was dismissed twice at Liu Xiang's request and reinstated twice. Or Liu Chengdong and Lai Xinhui, who were originally military commanders appointed by the central government, one was arbitrarily eliminated by Liu Wenhui, and the other was arbitrarily detained by Liu Xiang, and the central government ignored it. Even Liu Wenhui has twice sent telegrams opposing the central government, but because of Liu Xiang's recommendation, the central government has also twice ordered him to preside over provincial affairs. Other cases, such as the repeated conflicts between Li Jiayu, Luo Zezhou, and Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui, have also been regarded as normal by the central government, allowing them to live and die on their own. Under these circumstances, the Sichuan army's lack of fear of the central government is almost like Japan's lack of fear of the League of Nations. If the central government does not greatly strengthen its authority and restore its prestige, the Sichuan situation will never be resolved. This association believes that the people of Sichuan are innocent and have suffered from the pain of war every year. After careful consideration, we can only appeal to the central government for rescue. Therefore, we present two measures for your consideration and adoption: (1) Sichuan has neither communist disasters nor bandit troubles, and it has more than 2 million militia who can defend the area. There is no need to station troops there, especially since the stationed troops only scrape money and often have territorial disputes. To eliminate the scourge, the central government should immediately strictly order all the generals in Sichuan to transfer one-third of their more than 300,000 troops to Kangzang to consolidate the western border defense, and transfer two-thirds to Kuiwu to recover the lost territories in the east. If they fail to move within the deadline, the people should be ordered to stop supplying military expenses and grain. If they make excuses for lack of funds for departure, they can be asked where the funds for their mixed warfare come from. (2) If the previous order is ineffective, the central government should dismiss and punish all the generals involved in the mixed warfare, and send a senior official with military power to Sichuan to thoroughly reorganize the military together with the generals who obey the central government, in order to break up the defense zones and unify the Sichuan situation. If there are those who resist orders, an order should be issued allowing the militia to attack them. At this time, another major war may be inevitable, but using killing to stop killing is a last resort. As long as the central government can support the people and eliminate the warlords, even if there are significant sacrifices, we are happy to do so. The above two points may seem impractical at first glance, but we believe that in order to resolve the Sichuan issue today, unless such decisive measures are taken, no matter how much advice or mediation is given, it will be useless. Even if temporary peace is achieved, it cannot be maintained permanently. Moreover, if this situation of each dominating one side continues, the people of Sichuan may be wiped out. According to what this association knows, the strength of the Sichuan militia is more than enough to solve the warlords. The reason they dare not act is that they have no legitimacy or backing. If the government can support the people to solve the Sichuan issue, (1) Before the Sichuan situation is unified, each county can govern itself. (2) The militia of each county is allowed to drive out the abusive troops and maintain public security themselves. At the same time, A. The militia of each county will supervise all the people of the county to strengthen their defenses and not cooperate with the local stationed troops in any way. B. The elders of each county will strictly order their sons in the military to return to their hometowns with their weapons and be incorporated into the militia by the local authorities to take care of their livelihood. Then, all the warlords in Sichuan will collapse without a fight. In short, due to the development of the militia in Sichuan, the troops have become a burden. Their usual plundering of the people is already a heinous crime, and their current devastation of the local area is even more unbearable. This is what this association sincerely hopes that the government will quickly transfer the Sichuan army to rescue Tibet and resist Japan, and fundamentally eliminate the source of the chaos. In a situation of urgency and pressure, we send this telegram to cry out, hoping that the government will cut the Gordian knot with a swift knife and rescue the people of Sichuan from fire and water. This is our great wish. Sincerely, Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association, Yuan Yin.

Liu Xiang's representative in Shanghai received a telegram from Luo Zezhou on the 11th through Liu: "To Chongshi, Mingjie, and Zhenwu, my three brothers, confidential. Today at noon, I received an urgent telegram from Commander Luo of Wusheng. Chongqing Rehabilitation Supervisor Liu Jun, for your review. The national feud has not been avenged, and we are in extreme danger. We were hoping to sharpen our weapons and prepare to resist foreign aggression, but Liu Wenhui took advantage of the situation and claimed troops, attempting to annex. My department is unfortunate and bears the brunt. We have repeatedly retreated over the past few days. The facts are obvious, but enduring humiliation only prolongs the wickedness. Retreating only encourages his progress. Now I am forced to be stationed in Wucheng. The enemy is still besieging the city, and the flames of war have not ceased. Moreover, the enemy troops that were previously moved to Guang'an, Yuechi, and Hechuan are also successively gathering in the suburbs, with the intention of annihilating us. In this urgent situation, it is impossible to sit and wait for death. In addition to supervising the generals and soldiers to swear to coexist with Wucheng, I specifically and urgently submit this report, begging you to issue a decree immediately to stop them, or to intervene militarily, in order to cut off the source of the disaster. Wucheng will be fortunate, and the Sichuan situation will be fortunate. Luo Zezhou kowtows, Zhen. I hereby forward this message, Liu Xiangwen."

Radio Broadcasts During the Shandong War 145

▲Representatives from Twelve Counties in Jiaodong Send a Telegram to the National Government, Chairman Chiang, Acting Chairman Zhang, and Chairman Han Requesting the Transfer of Liu Zhennian's Troops to Suppress Bandits and Resist Foreign Aggression. The Telegram is Recorded as Follows:

"To the National Government in Nanjing, Chairman Chiang, Acting Chairman Zhang in Peiping, the Shanghai Anti-War Alliance, and Chairman Han in Jinan: It is found that Commander Liu Zhennian of the 21st Division has been stationed in Jiaodong for five years. His greed and tyranny are boundless, and the people dare to be angry but dare not speak out. Fortunately, hope is in sight, and we urgently call for help. We humbly present the sufferings of the people as follows: (1) Killing scholars to show power. Not long after Liu's troops arrived in Yantai during the Double Tenth Festival in 1928, they brutally killed party members and provincial government members Zhang Ruiting and gentry Zhang Ruixuan, along with more than a dozen others, and abandoned their bodies in the wilderness to demonstrate their power. The citizens were terrified. (2) Extorting donations on various pretexts. In 1929, under the pretext of suppressing Zhang Zongchang and Chu Yupu, a special donation was levied on the counties of Jiaodong, with small counties paying more than 100,000 yuan and large counties paying more than 300,000 yuan, totaling more than 2 million yuan. (3) Harsh allocation of supplies. Liu's troops originally received monthly salaries from the central government, but Liu still harshly allocated supplies to the counties of Jiaodong, under the guise of daily supply money, with small counties paying more than 10,000 yuan per month and large counties paying more than 30,000 yuan per month, totaling more than 3 million yuan per year, several times more than the land tax. (4) Abusing fines for opium and gambling. Instructing the county governments of Jiaodong and the public security bureaus of Yantai, Longkou, and Nanchang, he abused the name of banning opium and gambling to impose huge fines, ranging from tens of thousands of yuan to thousands of yuan, and even fabricated evidence and framed people. The amount of money confiscated for opium and gambling was used as the standard for assessing the performance of the county magistrates. (5) Controlling tax revenue. Whenever the country had affairs, he would seize the tax revenue agencies managed by the central government and the provincial government as his own, showing no regard for the government. There are cases to prove this. (6) Dividing administration. The county magistrates and bureau chiefs in Jiaodong were all appointed by Liu. They knew only of the division headquarters and not of the provincial government. The excessive taxation exhausted the people, who had nowhere to turn. Although Jiaodong was within the scope of provincial governance, it was no different from a foreign land. (7) Embezzling road funds. Except for the Yantai-Fushan and Yantai-Rongcheng road bureaus, which still belonged to the Construction Department, the remaining three lines of Yantai-Laiyang, Yantai-Muping, and Yantai-Haiyang were all built with funds extorted by Liu's troops, and all income went into his private pocket. (8) Forcibly seizing civilian property. North of Tongshen Village near Yantai and south of Qishan, he occupied more than 300 mu of civilian land in the name of a sports field, without paying any compensation. Moreover, in Yantai and other counties where troops were stationed, all the larger civilian houses were used as official residences for military officers without paying rent. (9) Brutally killing the innocent. If the people slightly resisted his greed and tyranny, he would accuse them of being counter-revolutionaries. In serious cases, he would burn and loot villages; in minor cases, he would arrest them and send them to the military court, where they would be tortured and die unjustly. The number of such deaths is countless. (10) Aircraft and warship special donation. Recently, he secretly ordered the counties in the defense area to collect a special donation of 80 yuan for every tael of silver in land tax, intending to purchase aircraft and warships to expand his territory. (11) Fabricating public opinion. The newspapers in Yantai were afraid of his power and dared not criticize him, but they did not help him either. Liu then started his own Donghai Daily to praise his merits and virtues, hoping to cover up the world's eyes and ears with one hand. (12) Forcibly conscripting soldiers. Liu had great ambitions and spared no effort to expand his troops. If recruitment was insufficient, he would forcibly conscript soldiers. Those who were conscripted often spent huge sums of money to seek release. Although Liu's troops have now withdrawn, they are still extorting and harassing the people in the areas of Ye, Lai, Qi, Hai, Mu, Wen, and Rong, making the people miserable. The troubles in Shandong are not over for the people of Lu; the people of Zheng are frightened by Bo You. If Liu's troops are not withdrawn for one day, the counties of Jiaodong will not be safe for one day. We urgently request that he be transferred quickly to save the people from fire and water, and at the same time, be used to suppress bandits and resist foreign aggression. Jiaodong will be fortunate, and the whole country will be fortunate. Wu Daguan, Ding Jianye, Zou Liquan, Yu Fangting, Liu Jiechen, Wang Daoming, Yu Weizhou, Gong Chengyun, Wang Chengting, Wang Zhongruo, Wang Xiantang, Cui Jie, etc., representatives from twelve counties in Jiaodong, respectfully submit this message. Winter."

"I have received your esteemed message and am deeply impressed by your earnest advice. Since the national crisis is becoming increasingly urgent, all those with blood and spirit are uniting to resist foreign aggression. However, Han Fu-chu is only seeking his own interests. He took advantage of the national crisis and the deployment of my troops to defend against foreign aggression to launch a surprise attack with his rapid telegrams. I only hope that the central government will issue orders to serve the country. I am willing to lay down my life for this cause. Sharp Decline in Exports to the United States in Nine Months 146

▲More Than 10 Million Yuan Less Than Last Year

According to the Continental Daily, statistics from the U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai show that China's exports to the United States in the first nine months of this year decreased by 75% compared to the same period last year. The value was only US$4,691,479, while the value for the same period last year was US$15,207,413, a difference of more than 10 million U.S. dollars, which is alarming. Moreover, it is found that among the exports to the United States in the first nine months of this year, the only item that increased compared to the same period last year was gold bars, with a value of US$18,792,818, an increase of approximately 2 million yuan compared to US$16,661,663 last year. However, this is an outflow of money rather than a real export of goods, and its value is not included in the aforementioned export amount. As for the export of goods, the most significant decrease was in inedible vegetable products, which were valued at US$358,946 in the same period last year, but only US$9,194 this year, a decrease of 35 times. In addition, the export of textiles and their raw materials, which used to be a major export, also decreased significantly in the first nine months, with a value of only US$1,858,124, compared to US$10,501,326 in the same period last year, a decrease of more than four times. In addition, inedible animal products decreased from US$9,945,920 in the same period last year to US$2,276,524. Among them, only ivory products increased from US$403 to US$1,070, which is a rare exception. Edible animals and their products also decreased from US$574,483 to US$100,968. Timber and paper decreased from US$31,934 to US$11,557. Non-metallic minerals decreased from US$112,022 to US$83,007. Metals and their manufactures decreased from US$202,684 to US$53,992. Chemical products decreased from US$13,627 to US$2,130. Miscellaneous goods such as books, maps, and works of art decreased from US$36,638 to US$13,781. Edible vegetable products also decreased from US$528,840 to US$282,202, but the decrease was the smallest. In addition, our country's exports to the Philippines and Honolulu have also decreased. It is estimated that in the quarter ending at the end of September, exports to the Philippines were valued at US$1,114,529, while in the same period last year, they were valued at US$1,814,826. Exports to Honolulu were valued at US$40,540, while in the same period last year, they were valued at US$61,570.

Telegram from the Northeast People's National Salvation Army 147

▲ A Bitter Account of Years of Warfare

▲ A Tearful Plea for Utmost Assistance

Cheng Yun, Chairman and Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army Committee, along with Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of the Heilongjiang Government, and more than forty commanders, including Feng Zhanhai, Wang Delin, and Li Haiqing, jointly telegraphed the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association in this city yesterday. They recounted the progress of the resistance against Japan. An excerpt from the original telegram is recorded below:

"The country is unfortunate; the brutal Japanese have invaded. Our three northeastern provinces have fallen for over a year now. Since the loss of Liaoning and Ningyuan, the enemy army has directly pressed toward Jilin, and provincial administration has been disrupted. We were then commissioned by the National Government to reorganize a legitimate provincial government, exercise political power, and accept the mission at a time of crisis and shock. We commanded the troops with utmost urgency, dedicating ourselves to the nation, unwavering in the face of setbacks. For the sake of convenient dispatch and coordination, the Jilin Provincial Government was temporarily moved to Binxian. Together with General Ma Zhanshan, we supervised the troops defending Heilongjiang, forming mutual support to contain the enemy army and launch a vigorous offensive. After several months of resistance, the enemy's courage was chilled. The powerful enemy mobilized the strength of several army corps to compete with us, taking advantage of the convenience of railway transport to encircle us. Our loyal soldiers fought bravely, each one matching a hundred. When ammunition was exhausted, they resorted to close combat, falling one after another, countless deaths, corpses piled up like mountains, blood staining the wilderness. The Japanese invaders, seeing that our will could not be shaken and our army could not be captured, resorted to

aerial bombardment, devastating our cities, injuring our innocent, and turning everything they reached into scorched earth. To avoid meaningless sacrifice and preserve permanent strength, I reluctantly followed the request of the merchants and withdrew from Binxian with tears. Subsequently, General Ma Zhanshan also withdrew from Heihe due to being isolated and without support. I and others are unable to defend the territory, and death would not be enough to atone for it. However, although the losses in the battles of Jilin and Heilongjiang were significant, the people's hearts were not dead, righteousness was widely proclaimed, and morale was boosted. Thus, the military and the people cooperated and jointly planned a long-term resistance, resulting in the organization of the Jilin-Heilongjiang People's National Salvation Army, with myself as the Commander-in-Chief. Subsequently, I telegraphed General Ma Zhanshan to rise again, vowing to make renewed efforts, and further collected able-bodied men from Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, launching simultaneous operations to expand the strength of the National Salvation Army. Within a few months, the National Salvation Armies of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang rose up, numbering 300,000. They were divided into twelve route armies, each responsible for a specific area, combining offense and defense.

Having struggled for half a year, the achievements of each army are not without merit. However, the headquarters of our army is constantly moving, and communication between the armies is often interrupted by the enemy, making information dissemination unreliable. Moreover, because we did not want the enemy to know our strength, and the enemy did not want the world to know that we still had a large base of operations in the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, the world knows little about the achievements of the National Salvation Army. In fact, the commanders fighting in the hinterland of Jilin and Heilongjiang and along the railway lines are making daily progress and fighting fiercely. This should be a cause for comfort to our compatriots at home and abroad. For example, Wang Delin, commander of the First Route Army, has recovered more than ten counties in eastern Jilin, fighting along the Jidun Railway, and completely destroyed the roadbed of the section from Huining to Dunhua, which was about to be built by the Japanese and was of utmost importance. All construction materials were burned, and sentries and plainclothes teams were recruited along the line to harass the enemy, so that the Japanese have not dared to start construction on that road until now and have not been able to complete it. Seizing the enemy's transportation and destroying the enemy's railway

has contributed significantly to the overall military situation in the Northeast. Li Haiqing, commander of the Second Route Army, fought thousands of miles, occupying Fuyu, Nong'an, Changling in Jilin Province, and Anda, Zhaodong, Zhaozhou, Lanxi, Qinggang in Heilongjiang Province, with a strong force. The powerful enemy has repeatedly suffered setbacks. Gong Bangjie, commander of the Sixth Route Army, has recovered Shuangcheng, Shulan, and other counties in Jilin Province, located in a strategic location, resisting the strong enemy along the southern line of the Middle East Railway, advancing without retreating. Deputy Commander Feng Zhanhai commanded even more elite troops, using both conventional and unconventional tactics, fighting thousands of miles from Fangzheng to Binxian, to Acheng, to Shulan, advancing rapidly. The enemy and traitorous forces were particularly fearful. Most recently, on September 12, he ordered the 5,000 soldiers under his command in the First Route Army, led by Gong Changhai, to attack Jilin City directly from Huanxiling, west of Ji City. They marched silently and arrived late at night. At that time, 2,000 Japanese soldiers in the city were densely deployed at the west gate, and they rose up to meet the attack. The vanguard of Gong's army arrived like sweeping away autumn leaves. More than 1,000 Japanese soldiers were killed, 600 were captured alive, and Colonel Juntian was killed in battle, resulting in a great defeat.

The puppet country's traitorous army collapsed upon hearing the news. The puppet governor Xi Qia also fled in a disheveled state. Gong's army completely recovered the provincial capital of Jilin City at dawn on the 13th. On one hand, they issued proclamations to reassure the people; on the other hand, they moved the army to the outer regions to prepare to meet the enemy, and blew up the railway along the Tumenling area of the Jichang Railway, cutting off traffic between Jilin and Changchun. The Japanese invaders and the puppet country were also cut off from communication. The enemy's arrogance was extinguished, and the puppet capital was shaken. The Japanese army was angry to hear the news of defeat and kept it secret. We are approaching step by step, and it can be expected that morale will be doubled and the entire territory will be recovered soon. Commander Ma Zhanshan still occupies Keshan, Heihe, Qingcheng, Suihua, and other counties in Heilongjiang Province, rising repeatedly, hoping to achieve the final victory. Commanders Li Du and Ding Chao's troops occupy Suifenhe, Hulin, Mishan, Baoqing, and other counties, forming a chain of defense. Other route armies of the National Salvation Army either adopt a plan to contain the Japanese invaders, organized into guerrilla forces, or take a coordinated combat approach, lurking

for alternating battles, like veins connecting smoothly, the arm serving the body, the finger serving the arm, like the Changshan formation, striking the head and the tail responds, striking the tail and the head responds. Although casualties are numerous, their righteousness is awe-inspiring. Gathering sand to measure rice is not enough to compare with their difficulty, and a rainbow piercing the sun is not enough to describe their fierceness. The beautiful rivers and mountains of Baishan and Heishui have not all fallen into the hands of others, thanks to the loyal and brave soldiers of the Liaoning-Jilin-Heilongjiang People's National Salvation Army, with their spirit swallowing the rivers and mountains, their righteousness reaching the clouds, and their hot blood filling the land. However, wherever the army goes, to ensure the entire army is vigorous, they must be well-fed. For sustained warfare, they must have an endless supply of food. The National Salvation Army has no support from the government above, lacks local financial resources below, has no internal replenishment, and lacks continuous external assistance. Barehanded, they shed blood and brains, and repay the country with utmost loyalty, relying only on hot blood and righteousness. In the spring and summer of this year, the timing and terrain were mostly unfavorable to the enemy's use of troops, and our National Salvation Armies were still able to use them as a shield. Now that the green gauze tents have fallen and the border region is cold first, in a blink of an eye,

the north wind is howling, and the accumulated snow is over the ankles. The National Salvation Army has no food for the night, no lined clothing, and no stored ammunition. How can they plan for complete security and avoid a desperate gamble with a tired crowd against a powerful enemy? It is chilling to speak of and terrifying to think of. This is why the establishment of the National Salvation Army Committee is for the purpose of boosting military morale internally and raising funds externally, which is extremely urgent. I and others, entrusted with the responsibility of the committee and entrusted with the hopes of the elders and disciples of the three provinces, undertake the arduous task and mismanage the army. In addition to supervising my subordinates to be more diligent and thoroughly loyal, vowing to do my best to restore the Northeast, fight for the country's honor, and seek survival for the nation, I respectfully inform the world of the experiences and hardships of our Liaoning-Jilin-Heilongjiang People's National Salvation Army, who hold their weapons to defend the country and fight hard for years. We hope that patriotic people at home, overseas compatriots, fearing that the national crisis has not yet ended, remembering that the future is difficult, and grieving for the suffering of the people in the Northeast, and for the National Salvation heroes who cut their throats and shed their brains to fight for this lifeline, will raise their voices and rise up with righteousness, either imitating Hongyang's contribution of wealth to save the border, or admiring Bu Shi's

sacrifice of family to relieve the national crisis, each exhausting their efforts, enthusiastically contributing, and jointly overcoming difficulties to protect our China. I hope that the masses will lift a heavy weight with ease, and the building will not collapse. This is what I and others dare to pray for with incense and tears, and to beg for on behalf of the people of the Northeast and the soldiers of the three armies. We hereby present our words, awaiting your clear instructions.

Cheng Yun, Chairman of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army Committee and Commander-in-Chief of the National Salvation Army; Deputy Chairman Deng Jianzhong, Shen Zhifu; Committee Member Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government; Deputy Commander Feng Zhanhai; Commanders of the National Salvation Army First Route Wang Delin, Second Route Li Haiqing, Third Route Jiang Zhongshan, Fourth Route Li Songtao, Fifth Route Wang Xiu, Sixth Route Gong Bangjie, Seventh Route Jiang Zhendong, Eighth Route Wu Caijing, Ninth Route Sun Leshan, Tenth Route Chu Jian, Eleventh Route Li Shaoxian, Twelfth Route Liu Pin, Fourteenth Route Zhang Guanghua; Committee Members Li Du, Fan Yunqing, Xu Zhen, Han Qinglun, Li Tianxiong, Zhao Zaitian, Zhao Guanmin, Han Chunxuan, Yang Boheng, Yang Zhiwen, Wang Zhijiang, Wang Zhenxian, Dong Qianmei, Zhang Yunzhong, Huang Mingxin, Liu Hongmin, Deng Mubin, Ding Maibo, Wu Lvgua, Lu Yunxuan, Yu Guangren, Ma Zhiqing, Jiang Zhichao, Deng Xiyuan, Chen Jiayi, Yin Jibing, Jia Pingzhou, Jiang Yunwu, Liang Jingzhai, and others, respectfully submit this.

Rectification of the Name of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army 148

▲ Northeast People Changed to Chinese People

▲ Overseas Chinese Volunteer Army Joins the 26th Route Army

Yang Yijie, representative of the Fourth Route Army of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Army, received a letter yesterday from Liu Zongyao, commander of the Fourth Detachment of the 26th Route Army, from Peiping, reporting that our Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army has now been renamed the Chinese People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army. In addition, Jiang Zihang and others of the Shanghai Songhu Anti-Japanese Overseas Chinese Volunteer Army, formerly in Shanghai, have been issued passports and official documents, and have been sincerely introduced to Commander Zhang Mingwu's subordinates. Jiang Zihang and others left Shanghai on September 28 and arrived in Peiping on October 4. They immediately went to the headquarters and were appointed by the commander as Lieutenant Colonel Commander of the Vanguard Team of the 26th Route Army. The others have all been given appropriate appointments. The official seals and appointment certificates were formally issued on October 8. The Vanguard Team is now undergoing rigorous training, eager to cross the border to kill the enemy, aiming to wipe out the Japanese invaders in one fell swoop. They also hope that patriotic compatriots across the country will unite in loyalty and bravery at this time of national crisis and fight the Japanese invaders to the death.

Furthermore, Liu Zongyao, fearing that bad people would impersonate the name of the army's representative to recruit soldiers in Shanghai, specially sent letters to various public organizations in Shanghai yesterday, stating that, "I am writing to inform you that I previously went south to request aid and was in contact with various parties. I then received a letter from General Commander Zhang of our route army calling me north to discuss military affairs. I did not dare to delay and went north. After arriving, I reported all matters in detail. The matters that were not completed in Shanghai have been temporarily handed over to Yang Yijie, the representative of the Fourth Route Army, for handling. After I have been fairly and publicly instructed by the General, I will have to go south again. I am especially afraid that unscrupulous elements will use the name of our route army to solicit donations or recruit soldiers to swindle people. Therefore, I specifically declare this, hoping that you will investigate and prevent impersonation, in order to maintain public friendship."

Yang Yijie Reports on the Anti-Japanese Situation of the Volunteer Army 149

▲ Recently Engaged in a Death Struggle with the Enemy

▲ Lack of Bullets and Cotton Clothing, Hoping for Assistance

Yang Yijie, representative of the Liaoning Volunteer Army Fourth Route, has been in Shanghai for more than ten days seeking assistance from the rear. He originally planned to invite people from all walks of life at the Youth Propaganda Group on Zhonghua Road at 2:00 PM yesterday to report on the recent situation of the Northeast Volunteer Army. However, because the address of the Youth Propaganda Group was inappropriate, the reception was changed to the office of the Northeast Volunteer Army Rescue Team at Sanmei Nunnery outside Xiaonanmen. A record of his report is as follows: (1) Recent situation of the Northeast Volunteer Army: Since the evening of September 28, the Japanese army has attacked Nanling in North Rehe with land and air forces. At that time, Li Fangting's 500 troops were surrounded by more than 1,000 Japanese puppet troops. Geng Jizhou received a telegram from Rehe in Jinxi and immediately led more than 2,000 cavalry to the rescue. On the 30th, he contacted the reinforcements of Li Li, Liu Gui, and Tang's troops and broke through several sections of the Jinzhao Road north of Yixian. We attacked on three routes, and the siege was lifted. At the same time, the enemy's return route was cut off, so they detoured through Yixian and retreated north. Geng Jizhou chased with cavalry and completely surrounded the enemy army in Erdahezi Forest. Liu Gui and Tang's troops also arrived. The enemy defended from a high position, and a stalemate lasted until about 7:00 AM on October 2. The enemy opened up reinforcements of more than 2,000 troops and launched a fierce attack with heavy artillery and aircraft, resulting in a fierce battle. Both sides suffered

Page 14

heavy casualties. Li Fangting's troops in our army lost a regimental commander, a battalion commander, and more than 300 soldiers. The enemy also suffered more than 400 casualties. More than 70 puppet troops surrendered. Our army captured four mortars, ten machine guns, and more than 200 rifles, all of which were obtained by Geng and Liu's troops. Now Geng Jizhou's troops are united with Liu Gui and Li Fangting's troops, planning to go north through Zhangwu and Tongliao through Tuquan to contact Ma Zhanshan's troops again, preparing for a long-term resistance. (2) Difficult situation of the Northeast Volunteer Army: Among the troops in western Liaoning who are determined to resist Japan, the only ones with strict organization and sufficient treasure strength are Zheng Jialin, Geng Jizhou, Li Fangting, and Liu Gui's four troops. Those whose front lines are at the forefront, all the bullets will be used up, and it is already snowing in the Northeast, so the climate is very cold, and each soldier is only wearing a single coat, and the food is only sorghum and millet, and there is no full meal. If assistance is not given early, in the near future, I am afraid that all the righteous soldiers will be bound to wait for death, so the greatest hope of the righteous soldiers at this time is nothing else but bullets and cotton clothing. I deeply hope that compatriots in the country will quickly rise up to assist and provide material donations so that the righteous soldiers outside the country can achieve their goals and recover the lost land."

The only ones who can fight the Japanese soldiers to the death are the volunteer soldiers. As for the combat situation of the volunteer soldiers, there is no need to say more. We and others, in view of the lack of people to rescue the righteous soldiers, initiated the organization of the Northeast Volunteer Army Rescue Team, hoping to raise medicines and other items in the short term and go north immediately to start rescue work, so as to fulfill the duty of the people a little. Recent News of the National Disaster Relief Team Organized by He Xiangning and Others 151

▲ Divided into Teams for Rescue After Crossing the Border

▲ Huangtuling Narrowly Escapes Forest Fire

Guomin News Agency reported that He Xiangning, Dun Junzhi, and others, in view of the fact that the Northeast Volunteer Army has been fighting bloodily for years and has suffered many casualties, have specially collected funds to organize a National Disaster Relief Team to go out to the rescue. The rear council of the team received a report stating that since the team followed Army Commander Peng Xiaoqiu out of the pass, the number of wounded soldiers seeking treatment along the way has been almost too many to handle. Therefore, wherever they went, they were warmly welcomed by the local people, who requested regular medical care. The team, considering that the righteous soldiers of the eastern provinces are scattered in various places, decided that if they do not divide into teams for rescue, it would be difficult to achieve universal results. Therefore, they set up a wounded soldier reception center with Peng's troops as the center, and are now working in Chelashanzi in the territory of Rehe. They also sent team members with Zheng Guilin, commander of the 48th Route Army, to stay in Huangshanling, Zixing City. A part of the personnel under Zhu Zhaiqing, the superintendent of the National Salvation Army, are also responsible. Recently, near Huangshanling, there were five enemy planes chasing the rescuers and throwing eight bombs in a row, all of which missed. The team members did not shrink back because of this. Now Army Commander Peng has ordered winter clothes for the team members in Peiping to be used in the severe winter.

Volunteer Army Support Association Aids the Volunteer Army's Clothing Expenses 152

Guowen News Agency reported that the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association has decided to allocate 20,000 yuan to aid the clothing expenses of the volunteer army. League of Nations Investigation Committee Report 155

▲ Full Text Published Yesterday

▲ Attachments Still Missing

The League of Nations Investigation Committee's Lytton Report was published in full yesterday, but the attachments are still missing. The report contains 228 pages in Chinese and 200 pages in English. Shanghai received 200 copies each of the Chinese and English versions, which were printed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Newspapers and public and private institutions will not receive complimentary copies. People in this city can purchase them from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at Fenglin Bridge. The Chinese version costs 6 jiao per copy, and the English version costs 1 yuan 2 jiao and 5 fen. The report has many attachments, and the details of the investigation committee's recommendations are also in the attachments. The documents the investigation committee referred to and the people they interviewed are also compiled into an index, all of which are important. Those who are concerned are eager to know the details, but unfortunately, they have not been published together. The general public feels regretful for not seeing the whole picture.

▲ There is a Saying He Will Go Abroad for Treatment

According to the Guowen News Agency, Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei has been ill and has come to Shanghai for treatment for over a month. Wang's external appearance is not bad, but he feels weak and powerless when walking. Two doctors from the UK and the US were invited by his wife, Chen Bijun, for diagnosis, and they are often in the hospital to diagnose Wang. As for Wang's departure abroad, I have only heard of it, but I don't know the details. Wang only notified the hospital to stay for another ten days and be discharged around the 23rd or 24th, and whether he will go abroad after being discharged and which country he will go to first are unknown. Discussion on the US Wheat Loan Issue 161

▲ Letter from the Five Provinces Farmers Relief Association to the US Consul General

The United Association of the Five Provinces (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei) Farmers Relief Association sent a letter to the US Consul General: "Dear Sir, We read in the newspaper that your Consul and the President of the Executive Yuan of our country, Song Ziwen, have agreed to a second renewal of the loan of a large amount of American wheat flour to China, which we heard with great surprise. Unfortunately, our country has suffered successive disasters in recent years. We are deeply grateful to your country for generously agreeing to provide loans for relief. However, because the amount of American wheat borrowed last year was too large and exceeded the needs of the disaster area, we had to sell it at a low price, which lowered the price of various grains. To this day, Anhui Province still has surplus relief flour that cannot be sold out. This year, all provinces in China have had bumper harvests, so the price of rice in various villages has fallen even more. In provinces such as Hunan and Anhui, the lowest price of rice is only a few jiao per yuan, and the price of rice is only three or four yuan (in the past three or four years, the price of rice has been over 20 yuan), so that farmers cannot afford the cost of farming. They are shutting down production one after another. Places without disasters are like disaster areas. This is all caused by the excessive amount of wheat flour last year. Now, if there is a continuation of this proposal, according to the newspaper, it will be 12 million US dollars, which is equivalent to about 500,000 tons of American wheat. Such a huge number is terrifying. If it is implemented in China, China's food will inevitably become surplus, the rural economy will be completely bankrupt, and farmers will have no way to make a living. They will inevitably become bandits. China is cracking down on the Communists. In this way, it will force the farmers to flow into communism. The future is dangerous and unbearable. In addition to sending a letter to our government to change its policy and find other funds, we specially write to you that if you need to borrow money, please cancel agricultural products and replace them with other goods, such as machinery, chemical products, etc., which are necessary for developing China's rich resources. Then it will be really beneficial to our country, and the people of China will be infinitely grateful. We venture to express our words. Please consider it carefully. Sincerely, The United Association of the Five Provinces (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei) Farmers Relief Association."

After the Northeastern Salt Tax Was Seized, the Ministry of Finance Still Paid Foreign Debt on Time 162

▲ But the Impact Is Great and We Are Seeking Ways to Remedy It

Since the fall of the Northeast, the salt tax outside the customs has also fallen into Japanese hands. The Ministry of Finance used the salt tax outside the customs as collateral for foreign debts to various countries. Since the tax revenue in the Northeast was seized, the Ministry of Finance, in order to maintain international credit, still paid it on time. According to financial circles in Shanghai, the tax revenue outside the customs can generate more than 10 million yuan each year. The national treasury has suffered a great loss due to this impact, so the Ministry of Finance has studied this issue and plans to find ways to remedy and deal with it.

Decision on the Distribution of Relief Funds for War Zones 164

▲ Each Lending Office Can Be Established Two Weeks After This Office

The War Zone Relief Committee of this city originally planned to use the 250,000 yuan of relief funds allocated to specifically handle the lending business in the war zone. However, due to the request of the secondary schools in the war zone that were affected by the disaster, 20,000 yuan was allocated to be used to relieve the secondary schools in the war zone that were affected by the disaster. The municipal commissioners of the disaster-stricken areas all believed that the general public had suffered huge losses due to the impact of the war this time, and they requested to increase the relief funds, which made it difficult to distribute. However, the committee still considered the actual situation and planned as a whole. Recently, it has completely decided on the distribution methods and lending procedures, and decided to convene municipal commissioners from the disaster-stricken areas at 9 am this morning to explain the various methods that the committee has decided to the municipal commissioners and urge them to actively prepare for the lending offices in their respective districts. According to the spokesperson of the committee, the lending offices and the lending sub-offices can be established and start lending in about two weeks. Recently, the general public has been requesting the Social Affairs Bureau for the increase of relief funds. Gu said that the lending office organized this time is directly under the Relief Committee and has nothing to do with the poverty lending office run by the Social Affairs Bureau.

Bo Wenwei's Opinion on Guiding the Huai River (Continued) 165

In the tenth year of the Republic of China, Wenwei returned to Shanghai from Hunan and discussed the issue of guiding the Huai River with the late Premier. The late Premier adopted Wenwei's proposal and included it in the Founding Strategy. It is the public opinion of Jiangsu and Anhui that the Huai River flows into the sea from the Guan River, and it has been reviewed and approved by the late Premier. At the second session of the fourth plenary session of the Central Executive Committee, Wenwei proposed a proposal on guiding the Huai River, and also adopted the opinions of the Jiangsu and Anhui Water Conservancy Association, and drafted a method description. The General Assembly decided and handed it over to the government for execution, but the executors of guiding the Huai River today have never considered Wenwei's proposal. Now, after reading the engineering plan issued by the Huai River Guidance Committee, it advocates guiding the Huai River into the Yangtze River. Since it is known that the Yangtze River cannot accommodate it, it claims to build a gate at the Sanhe Dam to limit the amount of floodwater flowing into the Yangtze River during floods, which is 6,000 cubic meters per second, which is 2,000 cubic meters less than the amount of Huai River flowing into the Yangtze River in the tenth year of the Republic of China. It is called guiding the Huai River, but it is actually storing water, which is already strange. It also claims to build flood embankments and use Hongze as a reservoir to increase its water level capacity for downstream irrigation and hydropower, which is even more terrifying. Reservoirs are advocated by modern engineers, but the upstream must be a sloping area and the downstream must also be a stepped area. Then choose the lowest-lying place and build it as a reservoir, so that the upstream and downstream can benefit from it. The current situation of the Huai River is just the opposite. The upstream Anhui-North Plain is only 13 to 15 meters above sea level. The average height of the bottom of the Huai River in Anhui is about 4 meters, and the bottom of Hongze Lake is 10 meters high, and the water level is more than 15 meters high. The Anhui-North Plain is already 2 meters below the Hongze water level. The ground in the lower He River and the Haizhou Salt River area downstream is 4 meters high. It can be seen that Hongze Lake is not a low-lying area in the upstream and downstream, but a high ground protruding from the upstream and downstream. The harm of the Huai River lies in this. If it is built as a reservoir, I, Yu, think it is definitely not a reservoir, but a water tower, which will inevitably irrigate Anhui and Henan in the upper reaches and breach Huaiyang in the lower reaches to cause a terrible disaster. Last year, the representatives of Anhui attended the meeting and argued according to reason, but the engineering plan issued by the Huai River Guidance Committee has not changed. Recently, Vice Chairman Zhuang also proposed to open up the abandoned Yellow River. It is heard that several million yuan has been raised for the project. The work of abandoning the Yellow River is difficult and costly. Even if billions of yuan are thrown in, it will be useless. American engineers have already said this, so the excavation of the abandoned Yellow River may also be a last resort for perfunctory calculations. Wenwei witnessed the disaster last year and knew that the disaster of the Huai River was becoming more and more urgent. Hundreds of thousands of miles of fertile land in the upper reaches had become barren land. The lowlands of Huaiyang in the lower reaches had begun to collapse and were about to be submerged in the ancient Si land. Jiangsu Province is following the old methods and only knows to block the mouths and repair the embankments. The design of the Huai River guidance team wants to stir up the waves, regardless of the lives and lands of tens of millions of people, for its scientific experiments. The people of the Huai River are ignorant and have never heard of it, which is sad. Guiding the Huai River is not as profound as science. It is just to follow the nature of the water and exit from the low-lying sea mouth. Then the obstacles in the middle stream can be scoured by the upstream water force and artificially excavated to form a new and orderly Huai River, so that the water can flow from the ground. Then the tributaries and ditches can be connected at the same time, just like the veins are connected, and the great benefits of the entire Huai River basin can be developed. If we still use the old wisdom of blocking the flow and building dams to form a high channel for the waste of water to come out of the Yellow River, Jiangsu Province may be spared for a while, but the agricultural benefits of the plains of Henan and Anhui will be lost forever. Wenwei has made many contributions to the opinions on guiding the Huai River since the first year of the Republic of China. Now, I would like to summarize it. A. The Huai River must first flow into the sea from the Guan River. B. The standard for guiding the Huai River is to reduce the current water level of Hongze. C. The design of the new Huai River must be based on the height and slope of the bottom of the Huai River in Anhui. It must slope down and there must be no obstacles in the middle. D. The bottom of Hongze Lake is higher than the upstream, so it cannot be used as a reservoir. E. The Huai River Guidance Committee does not have talents who are familiar with the water conservancy of the Huai River region. It should be reorganized as soon as possible. F. Guiding and reclaiming must be planned as a whole and cannot be divided into two things. A special bureau for guiding and reclaiming should be established to govern the water conservancy administration of the Huai River region to specialize in responsibility. After the guiding and reclaiming is completed, it should be transferred to the central and local agencies. G. Jiangsu, Anhui, Shandong, and Henan should jointly form a Huai River Guidance Association as a design and supervision agency. H. The cost of guiding should be borne by the land reclamation. The public debt should be raised after the cost of labor and the benefits of land reclamation have a definite budget and have been approved by the association. Foreign capital must not be borrowed first to prevent abuse. I. Guiding the Huai River must take into account the interests of the four provinces of Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, and Anhui and coordinate the overall situation. It must be fair and not just take care of one corner, harm other provinces, and treat neighbors as ditches. Everyone is selfish, and years of disputes have not been resolved. This is the biggest problem. I hope that the people of the four provinces will realize this as soon as possible and express their consistent opinions in order to save the past and prevent future disasters. Wenwei is very fortunate, and the Huai River region is very fortunate. Bo Wenwei Qi, October 10, 21st Year of the Republic.

Land Bureau Measures the Land in the Zikawei District 166

▲ Twenty-Eighth Bao, North Twelfth Map

Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau Proclamation No. 28: This bureau is now starting to measure the land in the twenty-eighth bao, north twelfth map of the Zikawei district. All landowners should pay attention to the following items: (1) The land chief will distribute the filling and reporting forms to the landowners. Each landowner should fill in the forms truthfully within ten days after receiving them, and the land chief will collect them and submit them to the No. 1 Measurement Team of this bureau, located next to the Guanyin Temple, east of the Anhe Temple Road, Zikawei Town, or the landowners can directly submit them to the measurement team. (2) If the landowner's address is unknown, so the filling and reporting form cannot be distributed and has not been received, you can go directly to this bureau or the No. 1 Measurement Team to fill in the form yourself. (3) If the landowner's land deed is mortgaged outside, so you cannot fill in the name of the land deed holder and the number of mu, you should quickly copy it from the mortgagee and do not shirk responsibility. (4) When the land of each household is measured, the landowner must, together with the land chief, clearly point out the boundaries to the investigators or surveyors, or entrust a representative in advance to point out the boundaries on site. Otherwise, this bureau will only rely on the land chief's instructions. If there are any errors in the future and disputes arise, the landowner will be responsible. The above four items are all related to the landowner's consolidation of property rights. In addition to informing the land chiefs of the map to abide by them, it is necessary to inform the public so that all landowners pay special attention to this proclamation. October 12, 21st year of the Republic of China. Director Jin Liren.

Foundry Industry Working Hours Trend, Social Affairs Bureau Approves Half-Hour Extension 171

▲ Orders the Guild to Persuade Factories to Proceed

All workers in the foundry industry in this city have been extending working hours by various capitalists in violation of labor-management agreements, resulting in labor unrest. The Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly convened capitalist guilds to advise them. According to the petition of the foundry industry trade union, the provisions of Article 3 of the industry's labor-management agreement regarding working hours are not fulfilled by most factories. Please verify." It is hereby verified that the Factory Law clearly stipulates that extending working hours requires payment of wages. Moreover, since an agreement has been signed, how can it be violated? Now the labor side is considering the current business difficulties and is willing to sacrifice half an hour of wages if necessary. If it does not exceed nine and a half hours, there is no need to pay extra wages. Its spirit of cooperation is deeply appreciated. However, the factories are greedy and have not yet agreed, which is very wrong. The previous situation has been reported again. It is appropriate to order you to immediately persuade the factories to strictly implement the methods set by the union to avoid disputes, and there must be no mistakes. The handling situation should also be reported back for investigation. This order is also approved for the union to be informed.

Public Document Strictly Prohibiting Tobacco Planting 172

▲ Officials Obey Orders Publicly But Disobey Them Privately, Military Law Will Be Enforced.

▲ Inspections Will Be Conducted Within the Territory of Each Province This Year.

The Shanghai County Government has respectfully received an order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, which was forwarded from the Provincial Government, stating that it had received a telegram from Chairman Chiang, saying that the provinces and counties disregarded the pros and cons and planted opium for a long time. Persisting in this self-destructive behavior would not only reduce food production but also harm people's health, inevitably leading to national collapse and racial extinction, leaving no hope for remedy. Every time he thought about it, he felt deeply grieved. Therefore, he hereby reiterates the strict prohibition, hoping that military and civilian officials at all levels will be inspired, work hard, and earnestly implement it, requiring all opium seedlings within the province to be eradicated and completely cleared within the time limit after the document arrives, and never be replanted. If anyone obeys orders publicly but disobeys them privately, or openly prohibits but secretly allows it, once discovered, the highest-ranking military officer stationed in the county and the county magistrate will be dealt with according to military law, and the provincial chairman will be punished for ordering private planting. In addition to ordering the Party and Government Committee of this department and consulting the central competent authority to first dispatch investigators to conduct on-the-spot inspections within the territory of each province this year and to conduct successive inspections, they are urgently ordered to strictly comply and instruct all subordinate county governments and military units stationed in each county to comply and publicize this to all. This matter concerns a specially ordered important policy, so do not neglect or violate it, lest it incur punishment. Therefore, the County Government, after receiving the order, yesterday issued instructions to all district chiefs and public security branch chiefs to strictly investigate and prohibit it and also publicized it to the residents of the county, informing everyone.

Completion of the New Building of the Special District Court 173

▲ Designed by Architect Yang Xiliu

In recent years, the First Special District Court of this port has been facing increasingly busy litigation affairs, and the original courthouse was insufficient. During his tenure, the former president of the court, Mr. Yang Zhaoyun, specifically requested funds from the Ministry to construct a new building. Since the current president, Mr. Zhou, took office, he has been actively promoting the project, which was completed last month. The Ministry of Justice sent personnel to inspect and accept the building, which was put into use this month. The building is a five-story steel-concrete structure, with a magnificent exterior and a spacious interior, including four large courtrooms, offices, lawyers' rooms, a repository for stolen goods, and a document storage room, all of which are quite complete. The total cost of construction was over 90,000 taels of silver, and it was designed by architect Yang Xiliu and built by the Renchang Construction Company.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Investigates Methods of Regulating Movies 174

The Shanghai Municipal Council, considering that there are still many points to consider regarding the movies currently being shown in the Settlement, even after inspection, specifically hired Mrs. A.M. Cannao, Mrs. P.C. Colman, and Mrs. A.E. Lunkley in April of this year to form an investigative committee to study the management of movies and the issue of movie inspection. The committee has held 15 meetings, summoned many witnesses to inquire about everything, and reviewed various suggestions and referenced methods from other places. The investigation has now been completed, and a report has been prepared and submitted to the Municipal Council. After receiving the report, the Council expressed its gratitude for the committee's hard work. The report is quite lengthy, and the following is a summary of its main points:

▲ Shortcomings of the Current System: The purpose of movie inspection is not to question the value of the content of the film, but only to ask whether it is suitable for public screening in the area. The current method of inspection is carried out by personnel from the police department, and the handling is still good, but it is too heavy a burden for low-ranking police officers to bear this responsibility, and the work is also very tight (an average of 50 full-length films and about 40 short films are inspected each month). Although there is an "International Inspection Committee," there is little contact with the inspectors of the police department. At the time of preview, no committee members are present because the number of committee members is too large, scattered, and powerless.

▲ Suggestion to Form Another Committee: The investigative committee advocates that a formal and powerful committee should be formed. Its organization should include one senior police officer each from the Public Concession and the French Concession, one representative from the Consular Body, one member jointly recommended by various women's public organizations, and one member each separately dispatched by the two concessions (preferably a legal, medical, or educational professional). When necessary, experts can be hired. Preliminary inspection should be carried out by personnel dispatched by the police departments of the two concessions (the two concessions must cooperate fully, and the right to approve or disapprove the screening must be in the hands of the two police chiefs). Each time a preview is held, in addition to the police department inspector, one member of the committee should be present. If the member does not agree with the police officer's decision, he or she may order the film to be resubmitted to the committee for review. The signed certificate of approval by the committee should be shown during the screening. As for the term of office of the committee members, it should be at least one year. Except for those who are concurrently serving as council members, their work should be rewarded. The investigative committee also suggests that the Municipal Council set up its own screening room to avoid the trouble of inspectors running around. The equipment for this room would cost about 60,000 taels of silver, but the cost can be covered by a slight entertainment tax or a handling fee.

▲ National Sentiment Should Be Considered: The investigative committee believes that it is difficult to set strict rules for the standards of inspection. However, in Shanghai, where people from all walks of life gather, special attention should be paid to the relationship of national sentiment. Furthermore, films that incite Easterners to despise Westerners or Westerners to despise Easterners must be carefully considered.

▲ Impact of Films on Young People: The investigative committee found that films of the bandit type have little impact on children, but films depicting sensuality are very harmful. The Chinese student class is greatly affected by them. Therefore, it is advocated that films be divided into two categories: one marked with the letter "U," which can be watched by everyone, and one marked with the letter "A," which is only for adults to watch. As for the age standard, it seems that 16 years old can also be used as a limit.

▲ Pictorial Advertisements Should Be Reformed: The huge pictorial advertisements posted by cinemas on the roadside are often overly exaggerated and often not very elegant. Although the cinema side first submits a reduced version of the advertisement to the inspector for review, the impression is very different between the large and small versions. The investigative committee suggests that all theaters stop using pictorial advertisements and use only text advertisements, at least for a trial period, to see if it affects the number of viewers. Also, the pictorial advertisements in newspapers can all be canceled.

▲ Improve the Content of Films: The value of films is not something that inspectors should overly concern themselves with. In the United States, there is a federation of women's clubs that publishes a film report every month, which is sufficient to indicate which films are not suitable for children to watch and which are suitable to watch. If this method is imitated in Shanghai, it will be effective in the long run. Also, in Australia, all film distributors must be registered, and if they violate the rules, their licenses can be revoked. Furthermore, the number of educational films currently shown in Shanghai is extremely small. The investigative committee believes that if this type of film is used as a short film and shown between newsreels and main films, it will be very beneficial to children.

In the appendix of the report, there is a written opinion from Chrisill and Hanah, representatives of the Film Federation, stating that the Municipal Council has no legal right to conduct inspections and that the Council has never inspected theaters and publications.

The Foreign Opinion Agency Issues a Statement 176

▲ Correcting Misinformation Regarding the Agency's News

Yesterday's newspaper reported that the Truth Bookstore was raided. It said that on August 27, the Public Security Bureau found the Truth Bookstore at No. 90 Messerdiro Road (corner of Rue Lupan), which specializes in selling Communist books and promoting Communist ideology. It sent a letter to the French police station, requesting assistance in the search and arrest, and stated that "the Foreign Opinion Translation Agency and the Theater Association are also affiliated to the bookstore upstairs and are both suspicious." The Foreign Opinion Translation Agency believes that this matter is of great concern to the agency's reputation and has issued a statement to correct the misinformation. The agency was established in early April and subleased the third floor of the building at the above address from the Theater Association. The Theater Association originally rented the space from the former Green House Tea Room. Later, when the Green House closed, a person named Xiao Shuzi subleased the storefront from the original owner and opened the Truth Bookstore. The agency and the Theater Association still deal directly with the original owner for rent payment based on the contractual relationship. The agency's personnel have a separate side door and have nothing to do with the Truth Bookstore. Moreover, the agency and the Theater Association were established before the bookstore, so the statement that they are affiliated with the bookstore is incorrect. The agency was established with the aim of introducing foreign opinions to make Chinese people understand the attitudes of foreigners so that they know how to deal with them. At the beginning of its establishment, it separately submitted reports to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the French Police Station for record and applied to the Municipal Government to consult the Ministry of Interior for registration. Since its publication, it has received the patronage and praise of party and state officials and social celebrities. The translated manuscripts are provided to newspapers, and central, provincial, and municipal party and government agencies have subscriptions (the Public Security Bureau also has a subscription). The scope of dissemination extends as far as Chahar, Suiyuan, Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, Guangxi, and Guizhou. The agency does not deny whether it is suspicious and is willing to make public all the manuscripts stored in the past six months for inspection to clarify the truth. According to news from the police station, when the Public Security Bureau sent investigator Zhou to the police station on that day and mentioned No. 90 Messerdiro Road, the police station immediately asked which of the thirteen households at No. 90 was involved. The person replied that it was only the Truth Bookstore on the ground floor. The police station then sent police detectives to accompany the search, so the feet of the search personnel did not step on the stairs. The agency's employees were able to enter and exit without any hindrance. The newspaper report is actually misinformation. Fearing that it will be spread and affect the agency's reputation, the agency has issued the above statement.
